<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows">"<i>I'll join <a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle" title="Tom Riddle">you</a> when <a href="/wiki/Hell" title="Hell">hell</a> freezes over! <a href="/wiki/Dumbledore%27s_Army" title="Dumbledore&#39;s Army">Dumbledore's Army</a>!</i>"</span></dd>
<dd>&#8212;Neville bravely rejects and protests against <a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle" title="Tom Riddle">Voldemort</a>'s offer to join him<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Deathly_Hallows" title="Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows">[src]</a></sup></dd>
<dd></dd></dl></div>
<p><b>Professor Neville Longbottom</b> (b. <a href="/wiki/30_July" title="30 July">30 July</a> <a href="/wiki/1980" title="1980">1980</a><sup id="cite_ref-birthday_1-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-birthday-1">&#91;1&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-ootp37_2-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-ootp37-2">&#91;2&#93;</a></sup>) was a <a href="/wiki/Great_Britain" title="Great Britain">British</a> <a href="/wiki/Pure-blood" title="Pure-blood">pure-blood</a><sup id="cite_ref-blood_3-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-blood-3">&#91;3&#93;</a></sup> <a href="/wiki/Wizardkind" title="Wizardkind">wizard</a>, the only child and son of <a href="/wiki/Frank_Longbottom" title="Frank Longbottom">Frank</a> and <a href="/wiki/Alice_Longbottom" title="Alice Longbottom">Alice Longbottom</a>. Neville's parents were well-respected <a href="/wiki/Auror" title="Auror">Aurors</a> and members of the original <a href="/wiki/Order_of_the_Phoenix" title="Order of the Phoenix">Order of the Phoenix</a> until they were tortured into insanity by <a href="/wiki/Bellatrix_Lestrange" title="Bellatrix Lestrange">Bellatrix Lestrange</a> and three other <a href="/wiki/Death_Eaters" title="Death Eaters">Death Eaters</a> with the <a href="/wiki/Cruciatus_Curse" title="Cruciatus Curse">Cruciatus Curse</a> when he was about sixteen months old. They were placed in the <a href="/wiki/Janus_Thickey_Ward" title="Janus Thickey Ward">Janus Thickey Ward</a> at <a href="/wiki/St_Mungo%27s_Hospital_for_Magical_Maladies_and_Injuries" title="St Mungo&#39;s Hospital for Magical Maladies and Injuries">St Mungo's Hospital for Magical Maladies and Injuries</a>, leaving Neville to be raised by his grandmother, <a href="/wiki/Augusta_Longbottom" title="Augusta Longbottom">Augusta Longbottom</a>. 
</p><p>Neville began school at <a href="/wiki/Hogwarts_School_of_Witchcraft_and_Wizardry" title="Hogwarts School of Witchcraft and Wizardry">Hogwarts School of Witchcraft and Wizardry</a> in <a href="/wiki/1991" title="1991">1991</a> and was sorted into <a href="/wiki/Gryffindor" title="Gryffindor">Gryffindor House</a>, along with <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter" title="Harry Potter">Harry Potter</a>, <a href="/wiki/Hermione_Granger" title="Hermione Granger">Hermione Granger</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Ronald_Weasley" title="Ronald Weasley">Ronald Weasley</a>. Throughout his school years, he was mostly a shy, clumsy, introverted boy who was constantly being told by his grandmother that he was not good enough or living up to his parents' accomplishments. However, in his later years, he showed that he possessed great courage and perseverance: he became an important member of <a href="/wiki/Dumbledore%27s_Army" title="Dumbledore&#39;s Army">Dumbledore's Army</a>, an organisation taught and led by <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter" title="Harry Potter">Harry Potter</a> with the goal of helping other students learn spells to attack and defend themselves. Neville would later fight in the <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_the_Department_of_Mysteries" title="Battle of the Department of Mysteries">Battle of the Department of Mysteries</a> (<a href="/wiki/1996" title="1996">1996</a>), the <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_the_Astronomy_Tower" title="Battle of the Astronomy Tower">Battle of the Astronomy Tower</a> (<a href="/wiki/1997" title="1997">1997</a>), and the <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_Hogwarts" title="Battle of Hogwarts">Battle of Hogwarts</a> (<a href="/wiki/1998" title="1998">1998</a>). During the Battle of Hogwarts, having refused Voldemort's invitation to join the Death Eaters, he destroyed the seventh and final <a href="/wiki/Horcrux" title="Horcrux">Horcrux</a> when he beheaded the snake <a href="/wiki/Nagini" title="Nagini">Nagini</a>. He also co-led the D.A. during his final year in opposition to the Death Eater professors. 
</p><p>After the end of the <a href="/wiki/Second_Wizarding_War" title="Second Wizarding War">Second Wizarding War</a>, Neville briefly served as an <a href="/wiki/Auror" title="Auror">Auror</a>, before becoming Hogwarts' <a href="/wiki/Professor" title="Professor">professor</a> of <a href="/wiki/Herbology" title="Herbology">Herbology</a> and marrying <a href="/wiki/Hannah_Abbott" title="Hannah Abbott">Hannah Abbott</a> from <a href="/wiki/Hufflepuff" title="Hufflepuff">Hufflepuff</a>. He is also the godfather of <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter" title="Harry Potter">Harry's</a> and <a href="/wiki/Ginny_Potter" class="mw-redirect" title="Ginny Potter">Ginny's</a> second son, <a href="/wiki/Albus_Potter" title="Albus Potter">Albus Potter</a>.   
</p>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Biography">Biography</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Neville_Longbottom?veaction=edit&amp;section=1" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Biography">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Neville_Longbottom?action=edit&amp;section=1" title="Edit section: Biography"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<h3><span id="Early_life_(1980-1991)"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Early_life_.281980-1991.29">Early life <span class="template-c">(1980-1991)</span></span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Neville_Longbottom?veaction=edit&amp;section=2" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Early life (1980-1991)">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Neville_Longbottom?action=edit&amp;section=2" title="Edit section: Early life (1980-1991)"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Order of the Phoenix">"<i>The one with the power to vanquish the Dark Lord approaches... Born to those who have thrice defied him, born as the seventh month dies...and the Dark Lord will mark him as his equal, but he will have power the Dark Lord knows not...and either must die at the hand of the other for neither can live while the other survives... The one with the power to vanquish the Dark Lord will be born as the seventh month dies.</i>"</span></dd>
<dd>&#8212;<a href="/wiki/Sybill_Trelawney%27s_first_prophecy" title="Sybill Trelawney&#39;s first prophecy">Sybill Trelawney's first prophecy</a><sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Order_of_the_Phoenix" title="Harry Potter and the Order of the Phoenix">[src]</a></sup></dd>
<dd></dd></dl></div>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 252px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/7/76/Longbottom_family_portrait.png/revision/latest?cb=20170730190047" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="250" height="145" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Longbottom family portrait.png" data-image-key="Longbottom_family_portrait.png" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/7/76/Longbottom_family_portrait.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20170730190047" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/7/76/Longbottom_family_portrait.png/revision/latest?cb=20170730190047" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/7/76/Longbottom_family_portrait.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20170730190047" decoding="async" width="250" height="145" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Longbottom family portrait.png" data-image-key="Longbottom_family_portrait.png" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/7/76/Longbottom_family_portrait.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20170730190047" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Longbottom_family_portrait.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Infant Neville with his mother and father</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Neville Longbottom was born on <a href="/wiki/30_July" title="30 July">30 July</a>, <a href="/wiki/1980" title="1980">1980</a>, to <a href="/wiki/Frank_Longbottom" title="Frank Longbottom">Frank</a> and <a href="/wiki/Alice_Longbottom" title="Alice Longbottom">Alice Longbottom</a>, a pair of <a href="/wiki/Auror" title="Auror">Aurors</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-birthday_1-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-birthday-1">&#91;1&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-ootp37_2-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-ootp37-2">&#91;2&#93;</a></sup> Moments after his birth, Neville was able to adjust his blankets so that he was swaddled more snugly, but no one witnessed this unusually precocious display of <a href="/wiki/Underage_magic" title="Underage magic">underage magic</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-PM-NevilleBirth_10-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-PM-NevilleBirth-10">&#91;10&#93;</a></sup> The midwife who attended the birth assumed that his father had tucked him in more tightly.<sup id="cite_ref-PM-NevilleBirth_10-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-PM-NevilleBirth-10">&#91;10&#93;</a></sup> Neville was born "several hours" before his classmate, Harry. 
</p><p>As a <a href="/wiki/Pure-blood" title="Pure-blood">pure-blood</a> wizard, he was likely related to other wizarding families such as the <a href="/wiki/Weasley_family" title="Weasley family">Weasleys</a>, <a href="/wiki/Crouch_family" title="Crouch family">Crouches</a>, <a href="/wiki/Potter_family" title="Potter family">Potters</a>, and the <a href="/wiki/House_of_Black" title="House of Black">Blacks</a>. Neville's parents were members of the <a href="/wiki/Order_of_the_Phoenix" title="Order of the Phoenix">Order of the Phoenix</a> and in these roles, they defied <a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle" title="Tom Riddle">Lord Voldemort</a> at least three times. Neville was one of two infants referred to in a prophecy made by <a href="/wiki/Sybill_Trelawney" title="Sybill Trelawney">Sybill Trelawney</a> about the person with the power to defeat the Dark Lord. The other was <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter" title="Harry Potter">Harry Potter</a>, and it was Harry whom Voldemort targeted on 31 October, 1981 making Harry his equal and leading to his first defeat.<sup id="cite_ref-ootp37_2-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-ootp37-2">&#91;2&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Shortly after, a handful of Voldemort's most loyal followers attacked the Longbottoms. Frank and Alice were tortured into insanity with the <a href="/wiki/Cruciatus_Curse" title="Cruciatus Curse">Cruciatus Curse</a> by <a href="/wiki/Death_Eaters" title="Death Eaters">Death Eaters</a> <a href="/wiki/Bellatrix_Lestrange" title="Bellatrix Lestrange">Bellatrix Lestrange</a>, her husband <a href="/wiki/Rodolphus_Lestrange" title="Rodolphus Lestrange">Rodolphus Lestrange</a>, her brother-in-law <a href="/wiki/Rabastan_Lestrange" title="Rabastan Lestrange">Rabastan Lestrange</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Bartemius_Crouch_Junior" title="Bartemius Crouch Junior">Barty Crouch Jnr</a>. The four Death Eaters were all sentenced to <a href="/wiki/Azkaban" title="Azkaban">Azkaban</a> for their crimes, while Frank and Alice were sent to <a href="/wiki/St_Mungo%27s_Hospital_for_Magical_Maladies_and_Injuries" title="St Mungo&#39;s Hospital for Magical Maladies and Injuries">St Mungo's Hospital</a>, where they would live the rest of their lives, not being able to recognise their own son. Neville was subsequently raised by his paternal grandmother, <a href="/wiki/Augusta_Longbottom" title="Augusta Longbottom">Augusta Longbottom</a>. At some point early in his life, he also witnessed the death of his grandfather.<sup id="cite_ref-GF30_11-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-GF30-11">&#91;11&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 252px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/a/a6/AugustaAndNeville1991.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20160408074805" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="250" height="210" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="AugustaAndNeville1991.jpg" data-image-key="AugustaAndNeville1991.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/a/a6/AugustaAndNeville1991.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20160408074805" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/a/a6/AugustaAndNeville1991.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20160408074805" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/a/a6/AugustaAndNeville1991.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20160408074805" decoding="async" width="250" height="210" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="AugustaAndNeville1991.jpg" data-image-key="AugustaAndNeville1991.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/a/a6/AugustaAndNeville1991.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20160408074805" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:AugustaAndNeville1991.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Neville with his grandmother at platform 9¾ before boarding the Hogwarts Express</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Neville's grandmother was a stern and formidable woman who was concerned when her grandson did not exhibit early signs of magic (Neville did, however, show faint signs of magic in him throughout his early years, something which his family persistently missed — the first such sign took place moments after birth, when Neville managed to magically shift his blankets more snugly over himself, something which went unnoticed by midwife who attended his mother<sup id="cite_ref-PM-NevilleBirth_10-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-PM-NevilleBirth-10">&#91;10&#93;</a></sup>). She often chided Neville for not living up to his family's honour and was partly the reason for Neville's lack of self-confidence early in his school years. 
</p><p>His relatives feared that Neville might be a <a href="/wiki/Squib" title="Squib">Squib</a>, though this was disproved when his great-uncle <a href="/wiki/Algie_Longbottom" title="Algie Longbottom">Algie</a> was holding him out of a window by his feet when he was offered some lemon meringue and let go. Miraculously, Neville bounced. Previous to this, there were various attempts to make him show signs of magic, including dropping him off Blackpool pier, where, according to Neville, he nearly drowned. Neville inherited his father's wand at the age of eleven when he started to attend Hogwarts. This wand was later broken during the <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_the_Department_of_Mysteries" title="Battle of the Department of Mysteries">Battle of the Department of Mysteries</a>.
</p>
<h3><span id="Hogwarts_years_(1991-1998)"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Hogwarts_years_.281991-1998.29">Hogwarts years <span class="template-c">(1991-1998)</span></span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Neville_Longbottom?veaction=edit&amp;section=3" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Hogwarts years (1991-1998)">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Neville_Longbottom?action=edit&amp;section=3" title="Edit section: Hogwarts years (1991-1998)"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="First_year">First year</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Neville_Longbottom?veaction=edit&amp;section=4" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: First year">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Neville_Longbottom?action=edit&amp;section=4" title="Edit section: First year"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Philosopher&#39;s Stone">"<i>You can't go out, you'll be caught again. Gryffindor will be in even more trouble... I won't let you do it. I'll — I'll fight you!</i>"</span></dd>
<dd>&#8212;Neville bravely standing up to his <a href="/wiki/Trio" title="Trio">friends</a><sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Philosopher%27s_Stone" title="Harry Potter and the Philosopher&#39;s Stone">[src]</a></sup></dd>
<dd></dd></dl></div>
<p>Neville began attending <a href="/wiki/Hogwarts_School_of_Witchcraft_and_Wizardry" title="Hogwarts School of Witchcraft and Wizardry">Hogwarts School of Witchcraft and Wizardry</a> on 1 September, 1991. While with his grandmother at <a href="/wiki/Platform_Nine_and_Three-Quarters" title="Platform Nine and Three-Quarters">platform 9¾</a>, he lost his toad <a href="/wiki/Trevor" title="Trevor">Trevor</a>. Once on the train, he met <a href="/wiki/Hermione_Granger" title="Hermione Granger">Hermione Granger</a>, who agreed to help him find his lost toad, and then <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter" title="Harry Potter">Harry Potter</a> and <a href="/wiki/Ronald_Weasley" title="Ronald Weasley">Ron Weasley</a> when he entered their compartment tearfully looking for Trevor. After arriving at <a href="/wiki/Hogsmeade_station" title="Hogsmeade station">Hogsmeade station</a>, Neville managed to retrieve his toad from <a href="/wiki/Rubeus_Hagrid" title="Rubeus Hagrid">Rubeus Hagrid</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-PS6_12-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-PS6-12">&#91;12&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 252px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/2/2c/Neville_being_Sorted.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20140921223031" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="250" height="127" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Neville being Sorted.jpg" data-image-key="Neville_being_Sorted.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/2/2c/Neville_being_Sorted.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20140921223031" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/2/2c/Neville_being_Sorted.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20140921223031" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/2/2c/Neville_being_Sorted.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20140921223031" decoding="async" width="250" height="127" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Neville being Sorted.jpg" data-image-key="Neville_being_Sorted.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/2/2c/Neville_being_Sorted.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20140921223031" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Neville_being_Sorted.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Neville being sorted in 1991</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Neville felt intimidated by Gryffindor's reputation for bravery. During the <a href="/wiki/Sorting_ceremony" title="Sorting ceremony">Sorting ceremony</a>, he silently argued for a long time to be placed in <a href="/wiki/Hufflepuff" title="Hufflepuff">Hufflepuff</a>, but the <a href="/wiki/Sorting_Hat" title="Sorting Hat">Sorting Hat</a> won in the end, and Sorted him into Gryffindor.<sup id="cite_ref-hatstall_13-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-hatstall-13">&#91;13&#93;</a></sup> Neville was so nervous that when the Sorting Hat shouted out his house, he ran across the <a href="/wiki/Great_Hall" title="Great Hall">Great Hall</a> with the Hat still on his head; he had to return to the stool to hand the Hat to the next student.<sup id="cite_ref-PS7_9-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-PS7-9">&#91;9&#93;</a></sup> On the way to Gryffindor Tower after the <a href="/wiki/Welcoming_Feast" title="Welcoming Feast">Welcoming Feast</a>, Neville had a bundle of walking sticks dropped on his head by <a href="/wiki/Peeves" title="Peeves">Peeves</a> the Poltergeist.
</p>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 252px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/1/1a/Flying_class_in_1991.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20161213051125" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="250" height="93" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Flying class in 1991.jpg" data-image-key="Flying_class_in_1991.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/1/1a/Flying_class_in_1991.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20161213051125" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/1/1a/Flying_class_in_1991.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20161213051125" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/1/1a/Flying_class_in_1991.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20161213051125" decoding="async" width="250" height="93" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Flying class in 1991.jpg" data-image-key="Flying_class_in_1991.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/1/1a/Flying_class_in_1991.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20161213051125" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Flying_class_in_1991.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Neville lost control of his broom during his first <a href="/wiki/Flying_(class)" title="Flying (class)">flying lesson</a></p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Much of his first year was plagued by similar mishaps. In his first <a href="/wiki/Potions_(class)" title="Potions (class)">Potions</a> lesson, Neville melted <a href="/wiki/Seamus_Finnigan" title="Seamus Finnigan">Seamus Finnigan</a>'s cauldron, and was subsequently drenched in the boil-curing potion they had been brewing.<sup id="cite_ref-PS8_14-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-PS8-14">&#91;14&#93;</a></sup> The following week, in his first flying lesson with <a href="/wiki/Rolanda_Hooch" title="Rolanda Hooch">Madam Hooch</a>, Neville accidentally broke his wrist after falling off his broom from a great height; afraid of being left behind on the ground, he had pushed off too early. He was taken to the hospital wing and his wrist was healed. Several hours later, he ended up heading to the <a href="/wiki/Trophy_Room" title="Trophy Room">Hogwarts Trophy Room</a> with Harry, Ron, and Hermione for Harry's duel with <a href="/wiki/Draco_Malfoy" title="Draco Malfoy">Draco Malfoy</a>. Nearly getting caught by Filch, they end up in the forbidden third floor corridor, where Neville drew Harry's attention to a giant three-headed dog. They manage to escape and safely return to Gryffindor Tower.<sup id="cite_ref-PS9_15-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-PS9-15">&#91;15&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>That year, Neville received a <a href="/wiki/Remembrall" title="Remembrall">Remembrall</a> from his grandmother as a gift which was flown in by an <a href="/wiki/Owl" title="Owl">owl</a>. This particular gift later allowed Harry Potter to become Gryffindor seeker. Draco Malfoy threw the small sphere into the air, and Harry flew to grab it, standing up for Neville. <a href="/wiki/Minerva_McGonagall" title="Minerva McGonagall">Minerva McGonagall</a> saw how easily Harry retrieved the ball and asked him to join the team.<sup id="cite_ref-PS9_15-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-PS9-15">&#91;15&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 252px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/9/93/Neville_Longbottom_under_the_effects_of_the_Leg-Locker_Curse.gif/revision/latest?cb=20140512182230" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="250" height="113" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Neville Longbottom under the effects of the Leg-Locker Curse.gif" data-image-key="Neville_Longbottom_under_the_effects_of_the_Leg-Locker_Curse.gif" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/9/93/Neville_Longbottom_under_the_effects_of_the_Leg-Locker_Curse.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20140512182230" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/9/93/Neville_Longbottom_under_the_effects_of_the_Leg-Locker_Curse.gif/revision/latest?cb=20140512182230" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/9/93/Neville_Longbottom_under_the_effects_of_the_Leg-Locker_Curse.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20140512182230" decoding="async" width="250" height="113" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Neville Longbottom under the effects of the Leg-Locker Curse.gif" data-image-key="Neville_Longbottom_under_the_effects_of_the_Leg-Locker_Curse.gif" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/9/93/Neville_Longbottom_under_the_effects_of_the_Leg-Locker_Curse.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20140512182230" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Neville_Longbottom_under_the_effects_of_the_Leg-Locker_Curse.gif" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Neville bunny-hops into the Great Hall under a <a href="/wiki/Leg-Locker_Curse" title="Leg-Locker Curse">Leg-Locker Curse</a> cast by Draco Malfoy</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Shortly after the Christmas holidays, Neville was the target of a cruel prank by Draco Malfoy, in which his legs were stuck together with the <a href="/wiki/Leg-Locker_Curse" title="Leg-Locker Curse">Leg-Locker Curse</a>. Neville had to bunny-hop all the way to <a href="/wiki/Gryffindor_Tower" title="Gryffindor Tower">Gryffindor Tower</a> so someone could perform the counter-curse. When Harry, Ron, and Hermione urged him to report Malfoy, Neville replied that he didn't want more trouble. Harry gave Neville his last <a href="/wiki/Chocolate_Frog" title="Chocolate Frog">Chocolate Frog</a> from Christmas and consoled him by telling that he was worth twelve Malfoys, and that the Sorting Hat chose him for Gryffindor, while Malfoy was in "<i>stinking <a href="/wiki/Slytherin" title="Slytherin">Slytherin</a></i>." Several seconds later, Neville inadvertently helped the trio identify <a href="/wiki/Nicolas_Flamel" title="Nicolas Flamel">Nicolas Flamel</a> when he gave Harry Dumbledore's collectible card from the Chocolate Frog.<sup id="cite_ref-PS13_16-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-PS13-16">&#91;16&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Neville was sent to the hospital wing a third time after a <a href="/wiki/Quidditch" title="Quidditch">Quidditch</a> match between Gryffindor and Hufflepuff. During the match, Malfoy began to taunt the <a href="/wiki/Gryffindor_Quidditch_team" title="Gryffindor Quidditch team">Gryffindor Quidditch team</a>, as well as Neville. Neville challenged Malfoy on hearing this, and single-handedly took on Malfoy's friends <a href="/wiki/Vincent_Crabbe" title="Vincent Crabbe">Vincent Crabbe</a> and <a href="/wiki/Gregory_Goyle" title="Gregory Goyle">Gregory Goyle</a>, while Ron fought Malfoy. Although he was knocked out by Crabbe and Goyle, <a href="/wiki/Poppy_Pomfrey" title="Poppy Pomfrey">Madam Pomfrey</a> insisted that Neville would make a full recovery. This was the first time that Neville stood up for himself.<sup id="cite_ref-PS14_17-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-PS14-17">&#91;17&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>In time, Neville learned about Harry and Hermione's attempt to take <a href="/wiki/Norberta" title="Norberta">Norbert</a> the <a href="/wiki/Norwegian_Ridgeback" title="Norwegian Ridgeback">Norwegian Ridgeback</a> up to the <a href="/wiki/Astronomy_Tower" title="Astronomy Tower">Astronomy Tower</a> to send to Ron's brother <a href="/wiki/Charles_Weasley" title="Charles Weasley">Charlie</a>. When he learned Malfoy was trying to get them caught, Neville snuck out of Gryffindor Tower to find them and warn them. He instead ended up getting caught by Professor McGonagall. He lost fifty House points, and was put in detention with Harry, Hermione, and Malfoy. Sent into the <a href="/wiki/Forbidden_Forest" title="Forbidden Forest">Forbidden Forest</a> with Hagrid to search for an injured unicorn, Neville and Malfoy went along one path with <a href="/wiki/Fang" title="Fang">Fang</a>, while the other three took another. When Malfoy snuck up behind Neville and grabbed him to scare him, Neville panicked and sent up wand sparks to warn Hagrid. When Hagrid learned the truth, he instead paired Neville with himself and Hermione.<sup id="cite_ref-PS15_18-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-PS15-18">&#91;18&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 222px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/3/37/PetrificusTotalus_PS.gif/revision/latest?cb=20161007222911" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="220" height="98" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="PetrificusTotalus PS.gif" data-image-key="PetrificusTotalus_PS.gif" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/3/37/PetrificusTotalus_PS.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/220?cb=20161007222911" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/3/37/PetrificusTotalus_PS.gif/revision/latest?cb=20161007222911" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/3/37/PetrificusTotalus_PS.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/220?cb=20161007222911" decoding="async" width="220" height="98" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="PetrificusTotalus PS.gif" data-image-key="PetrificusTotalus_PS.gif" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/3/37/PetrificusTotalus_PS.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/220?cb=20161007222911" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:PetrificusTotalus_PS.gif" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption"><a href="/wiki/Hermione_Granger" title="Hermione Granger">Hermione</a> casting the Full Body-Bind Curse on Neville</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>The night <a href="/wiki/Quirinus_Quirrell" title="Quirinus Quirrell">Quirinus Quirrell</a> attempted to steal the <a href="/wiki/Philosopher%27s_Stone" title="Philosopher&#39;s Stone">Philosopher's Stone</a>, Neville followed Harry's advice and attempted to stop Harry, Ron, and Hermione from sneaking out, though he did not know what they were trying to do. However, he thought that they should not be breaking rules and risking that Gryffindor would lose more points, and blocked the portrait hole, willing to fight them to make them stay. Hermione apologised and struck Neville with a <a href="/wiki/Full_Body-Bind_Curse" title="Full Body-Bind Curse">Full Body-Bind Curse</a> so that she, Harry, and Ron could leave. This was another early instance where Neville showed bravery, standing up to his only friends.<sup id="cite_ref-PS16_19-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-PS16-19">&#91;19&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>For standing up to the trio, Neville won ten points for <a href="/wiki/Gryffindor" title="Gryffindor">Gryffindor</a> at the end-of-term feast. Having moments before, tied Slytherin for the <a href="/wiki/House_Cup" title="House Cup">House Cup</a>, this pushed Gryffindor into undisputed first place. In the final exams, he scored well in <a href="/wiki/Herbology" title="Herbology">Herbology</a>, making up for his poor marks in Potions.<sup id="cite_ref-PS17_20-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-PS17-20">&#91;20&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Second_year">Second year</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Neville_Longbottom?veaction=edit&amp;section=5" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Second year">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Neville_Longbottom?action=edit&amp;section=5" title="Edit section: Second year"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Chamber of Secrets">"<i>You’d better open it, Ron. It’ll be worse if you don’t. My gran sent me one once, and I ignored it and — it was horrible.</i>"</span></dd>
<dd>&#8212;Neville telling Ron about Howlers<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Chamber_of_Secrets" title="Harry Potter and the Chamber of Secrets">[src]</a></sup></dd>
<dd></dd></dl></div>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 247px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/e/eb/PixiesWreakingHavoc.gif/revision/latest?cb=20140501113547" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="245" height="123" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="PixiesWreakingHavoc.gif" data-image-key="PixiesWreakingHavoc.gif" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/e/eb/PixiesWreakingHavoc.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/245?cb=20140501113547" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/e/eb/PixiesWreakingHavoc.gif/revision/latest?cb=20140501113547" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/e/eb/PixiesWreakingHavoc.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/245?cb=20140501113547" decoding="async" width="245" height="123" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="PixiesWreakingHavoc.gif" data-image-key="PixiesWreakingHavoc.gif" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/e/eb/PixiesWreakingHavoc.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/245?cb=20140501113547" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:PixiesWreakingHavoc.gif" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Neville and his classmates in Gilderoy Lockhart's first <a href="/wiki/Defence_Against_the_Dark_Arts" title="Defence Against the Dark Arts">Defence Against the Dark Arts</a> lesson</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>In <a href="/wiki/1992" title="1992">1992</a>, after the start-of-term feast, he applauded Harry and Ron for <a href="/wiki/Flying_Ford_Anglia" title="Flying Ford Anglia">flying a car</a> to Hogwarts. The following morning when Ron received a <a href="/wiki/Howler" title="Howler">Howler</a> from his mother, Neville warned him to open it quickly.<sup id="cite_ref-CS6_21-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-CS6-21">&#91;21&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>In <a href="/wiki/Gilderoy_Lockhart" title="Gilderoy Lockhart">Gilderoy Lockhart</a>'s first <a href="/wiki/Defence_Against_the_Dark_Arts" title="Defence Against the Dark Arts">Defence Against the Dark Arts</a> class, a pair of "freshly caught" <a href="/wiki/Pixie" title="Pixie">Cornish pixies</a> picked Neville up by the ears and hung him, by his cloak, from a chandelier. Moments later, he crashed back to the ground when the chandelier collapsed.<sup id="cite_ref-CS6_21-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-CS6-21">&#91;21&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>After the <a href="/wiki/Salazar_Slytherin%27s_Basilisk" class="mw-redirect" title="Salazar Slytherin&#39;s Basilisk">basilisk</a> attack on <a href="/wiki/Colin_Creevey" title="Colin Creevey">Colin Creevey</a>, Neville feared that he might be attacked, due to his poor <a href="/wiki/Magic" title="Magic">magical</a> skills, and tried to protect himself by purchasing a large, "<i>evil-smelling</i>" green onion, a <a href="/wiki/Pointed_purple_crystal" title="Pointed purple crystal">pointed purple crystal</a>, and a rotting newt tail. However the other students pointed out that Neville should be all right; he was a <a href="/wiki/Pure-blood" title="Pure-blood">pure-blood</a> and thus unlikely to be attacked. However, he thought he was very close to being a <a href="/wiki/Squib" title="Squib">Squib</a> and was still in danger anyway.<sup id="cite_ref-CS11_22-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-CS11-22">&#91;22&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 252px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/7/7e/B2C11M2_Great_Hall_Duelling_Club.png/revision/latest?cb=20161212010010" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="250" height="91" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="B2C11M2 Great Hall Duelling Club.png" data-image-key="B2C11M2_Great_Hall_Duelling_Club.png" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/7/7e/B2C11M2_Great_Hall_Duelling_Club.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20161212010010" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/7/7e/B2C11M2_Great_Hall_Duelling_Club.png/revision/latest?cb=20161212010010" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/7/7e/B2C11M2_Great_Hall_Duelling_Club.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20161212010010" decoding="async" width="250" height="91" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="B2C11M2 Great Hall Duelling Club.png" data-image-key="B2C11M2_Great_Hall_Duelling_Club.png" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/7/7e/B2C11M2_Great_Hall_Duelling_Club.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20161212010010" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:B2C11M2_Great_Hall_Duelling_Club.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">The first and last meeting of the Duelling Club that Neville attended</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Neville attended the first (and only) meeting of Lockhart's <a href="/wiki/Duelling_Club" title="Duelling Club">Duelling Club</a>. To practise the <a href="/wiki/Disarming_Charm" title="Disarming Charm">Disarming Charm</a>, Neville was paired with <a href="/wiki/Justin_Finch-Fletchley" title="Justin Finch-Fletchley">Justin Finch-Fletchley</a>. When Lockhart suggested the pair to volunteer spell blocking, Snape shot this down, claiming that Neville had difficulty with the simplest spells, and they would have to send what was left of Justin to the hospital wing in a matchbox.<sup id="cite_ref-CS11_22-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-CS11-22">&#91;22&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Shortly after <a href="/wiki/Valentine%27s_Day" title="Valentine&#39;s Day">Valentine's Day</a>, Neville informed Harry that his belongings had been searched by <a href="/wiki/Ginevra_Weasley" title="Ginevra Weasley">someone</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-CS14_23-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-CS14-23">&#91;23&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Neville would have been present at the end of term feast that year, having thankfully not been attacked or petrified by the Basilisk, and would have been present when all his classmates who had been petrified returned to full health after being cured by <a href="/wiki/Mandrake_Restorative_Draught" title="Mandrake Restorative Draught">Mandrake Restorative Draughts</a>, and would have been there to greet <a href="/wiki/Rubeus_Hagrid" title="Rubeus Hagrid">Rubeus Hagrid</a> following his release from <a href="/wiki/Azkaban" title="Azkaban">Azkaban</a>. 
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Third_year">Third year</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Neville_Longbottom?veaction=edit&amp;section=6" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Third year">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Neville_Longbottom?action=edit&amp;section=6" title="Edit section: Third year"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Prisoner of Azkaban"><b>Severus Snape</b>: "<i>Possibly no one's warned you, Lupin, but this class contains Neville Longbottom. I would advise you not to entrust him with anything difficult. Not unless <a href="/wiki/Hermione_Granger" title="Hermione Granger">Miss Granger</a> is hissing instructions in his ear.</i>"</span></dd>
<dd><b>Remus Lupin</b>: "<i>I was hoping that Neville would assist me with the first stage of the operation, and I am sure he will perform it admirably.</i>"</dd>
<dd>&#8212; A reference to Neville's skill as a wizard<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Prisoner_of_Azkaban" title="Harry Potter and the Prisoner of Azkaban">[src]</a></sup></dd></dl>
</div>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 252px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/4/4b/B3C5M7_Dementor_on_Hogwarts_Express.png/revision/latest?cb=20180424031501" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="250" height="89" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="B3C5M7 Dementor on Hogwarts Express.png" data-image-key="B3C5M7_Dementor_on_Hogwarts_Express.png" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/4/4b/B3C5M7_Dementor_on_Hogwarts_Express.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20180424031501" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/4/4b/B3C5M7_Dementor_on_Hogwarts_Express.png/revision/latest?cb=20180424031501" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/4/4b/B3C5M7_Dementor_on_Hogwarts_Express.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20180424031501" decoding="async" width="250" height="89" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="B3C5M7 Dementor on Hogwarts Express.png" data-image-key="B3C5M7_Dementor_on_Hogwarts_Express.png" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/4/4b/B3C5M7_Dementor_on_Hogwarts_Express.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20180424031501" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:B3C5M7_Dementor_on_Hogwarts_Express.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Dementors board the Hogwarts Express and enter the compartment that the <a href="/wiki/Trio" title="Trio">trio</a>, Neville, Ginny, and Professor Lupin are in</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>On the train ride to Hogwarts for his third year, Neville became alarmed when the <a href="/wiki/Hogwarts_Express" title="Hogwarts Express">Hogwarts Express</a> simply stopped. He entered the compartment Harry Potter, Hermione Granger, <a href="/wiki/Ronald_Weasley" title="Ronald Weasley">Ron</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Ginevra_Weasley" title="Ginevra Weasley">Ginny Weasley</a> were in to find out what had happened. A <a href="/wiki/Dementor" title="Dementor">Dementor</a> then entered the compartment, negatively affecting all the students within, though to varying degrees. Then new <a href="/wiki/Remus_Lupin" title="Remus Lupin">Professor Lupin</a> gave them chocolate telling them it would help them feel better about the shock. After arriving at <a href="/wiki/Hogsmeade" title="Hogsmeade">Hogsmeade</a> Station, Neville told people about the experience in the compartment.<sup id="cite_ref-PA5_24-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-PA5-24">&#91;24&#93;</a></sup> This made its way to <a href="/wiki/Draco_Malfoy" title="Draco Malfoy">Draco Malfoy</a>, who taunted Harry about fainting.<sup id="cite_ref-PA6_25-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-PA6-25">&#91;25&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>In their first <a href="/wiki/Divination" title="Divination">Divination</a> class, Neville accidentally broke two of <a href="/wiki/Sybill_Trelawney" title="Sybill Trelawney">Professor Trelawney</a>'s tea cups while reading tea leaves. As the class departed, Professor Trelawney warned him that he would be late next class and urged him to work hard to catch up with everyone else. In <a href="/wiki/Care_of_Magical_Creatures" title="Care of Magical Creatures">Care of Magical Creatures</a> class, Neville practised bowing to a <a href="/wiki/Hippogriff" title="Hippogriff">hippogriff</a>; he constantly backed away from the <a href="/wiki/Beast" title="Beast">beast</a>, which did not seem to want to bow back.<sup id="cite_ref-PA6_25-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-PA6-25">&#91;25&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>The next day in <a href="/wiki/Potions_(class)" title="Potions (class)">Potions</a>, Neville again managed to earn the ire of <a href="/wiki/Severus_Snape" title="Severus Snape">Professor Snape</a>. He somehow was able to turn his <a href="/wiki/Shrinking_Solution" title="Shrinking Solution">Shrinking Solution</a> orange instead of green. To ensure Neville would get the <a href="/wiki/Potion" title="Potion">potion</a> right, Snape told him that he would feed some of it to Neville's pet <a href="/wiki/Toad" title="Toad">toad</a>, <a href="/wiki/Trevor" title="Trevor">Trevor</a>, at the end of the class. Desperately, he asked Hermione for help; she whispered instructions to him out of the corner of her mouth. By the end of class, he was able to turn his potion green, and successfully shrunk Trevor from a toad to a tadpole. Upon returning Trevor to his proper size, Snape took five points from Hermione simply to spite the <a href="/wiki/Gryffindor" title="Gryffindor">Gryffindors</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-PA7_7-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-PA7-7">&#91;7&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 222px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/b/b6/Neville%27s_boggart.gif/revision/latest?cb=20190402102559" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="220" height="92" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Neville&#39;s boggart.gif" data-image-key="Neville&#39;s_boggart.gif" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/b/b6/Neville%27s_boggart.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/220?cb=20190402102559" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/b/b6/Neville%27s_boggart.gif/revision/latest?cb=20190402102559" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/b/b6/Neville%27s_boggart.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/220?cb=20190402102559" decoding="async" width="220" height="92" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Neville&#39;s boggart.gif" data-image-key="Neville&#39;s_boggart.gif" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/b/b6/Neville%27s_boggart.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/220?cb=20190402102559" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Neville%27s_boggart.gif" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Neville's <a href="/wiki/Boggart" title="Boggart">Boggart</a>, <a href="/wiki/Severus_Snape" title="Severus Snape">Professor Snape</a></p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Later that day, Neville helped Professor Remus Lupin's first practical <a href="/wiki/Defence_Against_the_Dark_Arts" title="Defence Against the Dark Arts">Defence Against the Dark Arts</a> lesson about boggarts. Neville was the first person to be asked. This was most likely because of Professor Lupin's preference for the underdog and him wanting to build Neville's confidence. When asked what scared him most in the world, Neville replied "<i>Professor Snape</i>", to which everyone found amusing. To counter the boggart, Lupin asked Neville to picture Snape in his grandmother's clothes. For his help, Neville earned ten points for Gryffindor and he confidently banished the boggart at the end of class.<sup id="cite_ref-PA7_7-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-PA7-7">&#91;7&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 252px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/1/18/Gryffindor_common_room_1993.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20150729002112" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="250" height="106" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Gryffindor common room 1993.jpg" data-image-key="Gryffindor_common_room_1993.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/1/18/Gryffindor_common_room_1993.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20150729002112" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/1/18/Gryffindor_common_room_1993.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20150729002112" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/1/18/Gryffindor_common_room_1993.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20150729002112" decoding="async" width="250" height="106" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Gryffindor common room 1993.jpg" data-image-key="Gryffindor_common_room_1993.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/1/18/Gryffindor_common_room_1993.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20150729002112" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Gryffindor_common_room_1993.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Professor McGonagall and the residents of <a href="/wiki/Gryffindor_Tower" title="Gryffindor Tower">Gryffindor Tower</a> in the common room after Sirius Black's break-in</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>In the spring of <a href="/wiki/1994" title="1994">1994</a>, Neville lost the passwords to <a href="/wiki/Gryffindor_Tower" title="Gryffindor Tower">Gryffindor Tower</a>; because <a href="/wiki/Cadogan" title="Cadogan">Sir Cadogan</a> changed them so frequently, Neville needed to write them down so he could remember them.<sup id="cite_ref-PA12_26-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-PA12-26">&#91;26&#93;</a></sup> After the passwords disappeared, <a href="/wiki/Sirius_Black" title="Sirius Black">Sirius Black</a> managed to enter Gryffindor Tower with a knife. After learning Neville was indirectly responsible, Professor McGonagall banned him from all future visits into <a href="/wiki/Hogsmeade" title="Hogsmeade">Hogsmeade</a> for the remainder of the school year, gave him a detention, and forbade anyone from giving him the password to the common room, thus he had to wait outside the portrait until someone came by while security trolls hired to guard the Fat Lady leered unpleasantly at him. But none of that compared to what his grandmother had in store for him. Two days later during breakfast, Neville received a <a href="/wiki/Howler" title="Howler">Howler</a> from her; he tore out of the <a href="/wiki/Great_Hall" title="Great Hall">Great Hall</a>, amid shouts of laughter, and opened it in the <a href="/wiki/Entrance_Hall" title="Entrance Hall">Entrance Hall</a>, where his grandmother's angry voice told him he brought shame to their family.<sup id="cite_ref-PA14_27-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-PA14-27">&#91;27&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>At the end of his Divination final exam, Neville was told that, if he told anyone his results, he would suffer a serious accident.<sup id="cite_ref-PA16_28-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-PA16-28">&#91;28&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Fourth_year">Fourth year</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Neville_Longbottom?veaction=edit&amp;section=7" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Fourth year">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Neville_Longbottom?action=edit&amp;section=7" title="Edit section: Fourth year"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Goblet of Fire"><b>Hermione Granger</b>: "<i>Neville, are you all right?</i>"</span></dd>
<dd><b>Neville</b>: "<i>Oh, yes, I'm fine. Very interesting dinner — I mean lesson — what's for eating?</i>"</dd>
<dd>&#8212; Neville in an "unnaturally high voice" after a lesson on the Unforgivable Curses<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Goblet_of_Fire" title="Harry Potter and the Goblet of Fire">[src]</a></sup></dd></dl>
</div>
<p>In 1994, Neville met up with Harry, Ron, and Hermione on the <a href="/wiki/Hogwarts_Express" title="Hogwarts Express">Hogwarts Express</a>. He jealously listened to their recap of the <a href="/wiki/Quidditch_World_Cup" title="Quidditch World Cup">Quidditch World Cup</a>; his grandmother had not wanted to go, and did not purchase tickets.<sup id="cite_ref-GF11_29-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-GF11-29">&#91;29&#93;</a></sup> He was also awestruck by Ron's miniature figurine of Viktor Krum.<sup id="cite_ref-GF11_29-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-GF11-29">&#91;29&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 252px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/8/8b/Fourth_year_DADA.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20150723223201" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="250" height="120" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Fourth year DADA.jpg" data-image-key="Fourth_year_DADA.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/8/8b/Fourth_year_DADA.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20150723223201" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/8/8b/Fourth_year_DADA.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20150723223201" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/8/8b/Fourth_year_DADA.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20150723223201" decoding="async" width="250" height="120" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Fourth year DADA.jpg" data-image-key="Fourth_year_DADA.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/8/8b/Fourth_year_DADA.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20150723223201" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Fourth_year_DADA.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">"Moody" demonstrating the <a href="/wiki/Cruciatus_Curse" title="Cruciatus Curse">Cruciatus Curse</a> on a spider</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>In <a href="/wiki/Alastor_Moody" title="Alastor Moody">"Mad-Eye" Moody</a>'s first <a href="/wiki/Defence_Against_the_Dark_Arts" title="Defence Against the Dark Arts">Defence Against the Dark Arts</a> class, Neville was able to supply information about the <a href="/wiki/Unforgivable_Curses" title="Unforgivable Curses">Unforgivable Curses</a>, in particular the <a href="/wiki/Cruciatus_Curse" title="Cruciatus Curse">Cruciatus Curse</a>. When Moody demonstrated the curse on a spider, Neville was terrified; he gripped his desk so hard, his knuckles turned white. Hermione noticed this and called for the professor to stop. After class, Moody — who was in fact <a href="/wiki/Bartemius_Crouch_Junior" title="Bartemius Crouch Junior">Barty Crouch Jnr</a>, one of the attackers of Neville's parents, under disguise by use of <a href="/wiki/Polyjuice_Potion" title="Polyjuice Potion">Polyjuice Potion</a> — took Neville to his office for a cup of tea.
</p><p>Having heard from <a href="/wiki/Pomona_Sprout" title="Pomona Sprout">Professor Sprout</a> about Neville's aptitude in <a href="/wiki/Herbology" title="Herbology">Herbology</a>, Moody cheered Neville up by telling him what Sprout had said and gave him a number of books he thought Neville would enjoy. One of them was <i><a href="/wiki/Magical_Mediterranean_Water-Plants_and_Their_Properties" title="Magical Mediterranean Water-Plants and Their Properties">Magical Water Plants of the Mediterranean</a></i>, which Crouch intended for Harry to read in order to learn all about <a href="/wiki/Gillyweed" title="Gillyweed">Gillyweed</a> for the second task<sup id="cite_ref-GF14_30-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-GF14-30">&#91;30&#93;</a></sup>, but he was stubbornly searching through the library.<sup id="cite_ref-GF26_31-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-GF26-31">&#91;31&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>A few days later in class, Neville was put under the <a href="/wiki/Imperius_Curse" title="Imperius Curse">Imperius Curse</a> by Moody, under the pretence of letting the class know what it felt like. Under Moody's influence, Neville performed a series of "<i>quite astonishing gymnastics</i>" that he could not have performed normally.<sup id="cite_ref-GF15_32-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-GF15-32">&#91;32&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 247px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/b/bc/Yule_ball2.gif/revision/latest?cb=20140921221911" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="245" height="120" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Yule ball2.gif" data-image-key="Yule_ball2.gif" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/b/bc/Yule_ball2.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/245?cb=20140921221911" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/b/bc/Yule_ball2.gif/revision/latest?cb=20140921221911" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/b/bc/Yule_ball2.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/245?cb=20140921221911" decoding="async" width="245" height="120" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Yule ball2.gif" data-image-key="Yule_ball2.gif" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/b/bc/Yule_ball2.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/245?cb=20140921221911" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Yule_ball2.gif" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Neville and Ginny Weasley at the <a href="/wiki/Yule_Ball" title="Yule Ball">Yule Ball</a></p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>When the Yule Ball was announced during the <a href="/wiki/Triwizard_Tournament" title="Triwizard Tournament">Triwizard Tournament</a>, Neville asked Hermione to go with him. After Hermione politely declined, having already agreed to attend with <a href="/wiki/Viktor_Krum" title="Viktor Krum">Viktor Krum</a>, Neville asked <a href="/wiki/Ginevra_Weasley" title="Ginevra Weasley">Ginny Weasley</a>. While the pair seemed to enjoy themselves, Neville accidentally stepped on Ginny's toes while dancing.<sup id="cite_ref-GF23_33-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-GF23-33">&#91;33&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>It can be assumed that Neville was among the spectators of the third task ( <a href="/wiki/Triwizard_Maze" title="Triwizard Maze">Triwizard Maze</a>), supporting Harry along with his fellow Gryffindors. He was also most likely among the mass of students that attended the <a href="/wiki/Memorial_feast_to_Cedric_Diggory" title="Memorial feast to Cedric Diggory">Memorial feast to Cedric Diggory</a>, after Cedric was murdered on the orders of Lord Voldemort.
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Fifth_year">Fifth year</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Neville_Longbottom?veaction=edit&amp;section=8" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Fifth year">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Neville_Longbottom?action=edit&amp;section=8" title="Edit section: Fifth year"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Order of the Phoenix"><b>Neville</b>: "<i>We were all in the D.A. together. It was all supposed to be about fighting You-Know-Who, wasn't it? And this is the first chance we've had to do something real — or was that all just a game or something?</i>"</span></dd>
<dd><b>Harry Potter</b>: "<i>No — of course it wasn't —</i>"</dd>
<dd><b>Neville</b>: "<i>Then we should come too. We want to help.</i>"</dd>
<dd>&#8212; Neville insists on going with the trio to the <a href="/wiki/Department_of_Mysteries" title="Department of Mysteries">Department of Mysteries</a><sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Order_of_the_Phoenix" title="Harry Potter and the Order of the Phoenix">[src]</a></sup></dd></dl>
</div>
<p>In 1995, Neville met with Harry and Ginny on the Hogwarts Express. Searching for seats, the trio entered <a href="/wiki/Luna_Lovegood" title="Luna Lovegood">Luna Lovegood</a>'s compartment. Once inside, he excitedly showed them his <a href="/wiki/Mimbulus_mimbletonia" title="Mimbulus mimbletonia">Mimbulus mimbletonia</a>, a birthday present from his <a href="/wiki/Algie" class="mw-redirect" title="Algie">great-uncle Algie</a>. He told them about his plans to show it to Professor Sprout, as well as wanting to breed it.<sup id="cite_ref-OP10_34-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-OP10-34">&#91;34&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>After arriving at Hogwarts, Neville helped Harry get into Gryffindor Tower as Harry had not learned the new password yet, and then defended Harry during a verbal fight with <a href="/wiki/Seamus_Finnigan" title="Seamus Finnigan">Seamus Finnigan</a>, claiming that the <i><a href="/wiki/Daily_Prophet" title="Daily Prophet">Daily Prophet</a></i> was going downhill, not Harry and Dumbledore. He and his grandmother both believed Harry's claim that Voldemort had returned, and had cancelled their subscription to the newspaper.<sup id="cite_ref-OP11_35-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-OP11-35">&#91;35&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 252px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/3/3b/OOTP_DA_Neville_Disarming_Parvati.gif/revision/latest?cb=20161007212600" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="250" height="111" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="OOTP DA Neville Disarming Parvati.gif" data-image-key="OOTP_DA_Neville_Disarming_Parvati.gif" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/3/3b/OOTP_DA_Neville_Disarming_Parvati.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20161007212600" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/3/3b/OOTP_DA_Neville_Disarming_Parvati.gif/revision/latest?cb=20161007212600" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/3/3b/OOTP_DA_Neville_Disarming_Parvati.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20161007212600" decoding="async" width="250" height="111" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="OOTP DA Neville Disarming Parvati.gif" data-image-key="OOTP_DA_Neville_Disarming_Parvati.gif" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/3/3b/OOTP_DA_Neville_Disarming_Parvati.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20161007212600" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:OOTP_DA_Neville_Disarming_Parvati.gif" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Neville finally masters the Disarming Charm during a D.A. meeting</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>When Harry, Ron, and Hermione began organising <a href="/wiki/Dumbledore%27s_Army" title="Dumbledore&#39;s Army">Dumbledore's Army</a>, Neville was among the first to sign up. At their first meeting in the <a href="/wiki/Room_of_Requirement" title="Room of Requirement">Room of Requirement</a>, Neville was left partner-less when they began practice; Neville instead partnered with Harry. After successfully disarming Harry, Neville then joined Ron and Hermione, so Harry could check on the others.<sup id="cite_ref-OP18_36-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-OP18-36">&#91;36&#93;</a></sup> With Harry's encouragement, by the beginning of Christmas break, Neville had improved "<i>beyond all recognition</i>."<sup id="cite_ref-OP21_37-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-OP21-37">&#91;37&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 252px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/9/9e/StMungos_PM_B5C23M1_ChristmasAtStMungos_Moment.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20201109221209" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="250" height="102" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="StMungos PM B5C23M1 ChristmasAtStMungos Moment.jpg" data-image-key="StMungos_PM_B5C23M1_ChristmasAtStMungos_Moment.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/9/9e/StMungos_PM_B5C23M1_ChristmasAtStMungos_Moment.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20201109221209" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/9/9e/StMungos_PM_B5C23M1_ChristmasAtStMungos_Moment.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20201109221209" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/9/9e/StMungos_PM_B5C23M1_ChristmasAtStMungos_Moment.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20201109221209" decoding="async" width="250" height="102" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="StMungos PM B5C23M1 ChristmasAtStMungos Moment.jpg" data-image-key="StMungos_PM_B5C23M1_ChristmasAtStMungos_Moment.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/9/9e/StMungos_PM_B5C23M1_ChristmasAtStMungos_Moment.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20201109221209" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:StMungos_PM_B5C23M1_ChristmasAtStMungos_Moment.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Neville and his grandmother visiting St Mungo's</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>During Christmas break, Ron, Hermione, and Ginny learned that Neville's parents were not dead, but patients in <a href="/wiki/St_Mungo%27s_Hospital_for_Magical_Maladies_and_Injuries" title="St Mungo&#39;s Hospital for Magical Maladies and Injuries">St Mungo's Hospital for Magical Maladies and Injuries</a>, having gone insane after being tortured by a group of Death Eaters at the end of the <a href="/wiki/First_Wizarding_War" title="First Wizarding War">First Wizarding War</a>. Harry was the only one who already knew this, having found out in the <a href="/wiki/Pensieve" title="Pensieve">Pensieve</a> in 1994, but he had told no one, keeping Neville's secret safe. Before Neville left, his mother handed him an empty Droobles Blowing Gum wrapper; while his grandmother wanted him to throw it away, Neville instead pocketed it.<sup id="cite_ref-OP23_38-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-OP23-38">&#91;38&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>When it was learned that ten <a href="/wiki/Death_Eaters" title="Death Eaters">Death Eaters</a> escaped from Azkaban in 1996, including three of the ones responsible for the torture of Neville's parents, Neville did not speak of it, but it "<i>wrought a strange and even slightly alarming change</i>" in him, according to Harry. He worked harder than anyone in D.A. meetings, and was the fastest to pick up new spells aside from Hermione.<sup id="cite_ref-OP25_39-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-OP25-39">&#91;39&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>When on <a href="/wiki/18_June" title="18 June">18 June</a> Harry had a vision that <a href="/wiki/Sirius_Black" title="Sirius Black">Sirius Black</a> was tortured by Voldemort in the Department of Mysteries at the <a href="/wiki/British_Ministry_of_Magic" title="British Ministry of Magic">Ministry of Magic</a>, he informed Ron and Hermione. The latter convinced Harry to check to see if Sirius was at <a href="/wiki/12_Grimmauld_Place" title="12 Grimmauld Place">12 Grimmauld Place</a> before rushing off to rescue him, and Ginny and Luna came to their assistance. Harry and Hermione broke into Umbridge's office, and Ron wanted to trick Umbridge, Ginny and Luna stopped people from entering the corridor. Umbridge unfortunately wasn't fooled and ordered the <a href="/wiki/Inquisitorial_Squad" title="Inquisitorial Squad">Inquisitorial Squad</a> to round them up. Neville, seeing what is going on, tried to help, but he was caught as well.<sup id="cite_ref-OP32_40-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-OP32-40">&#91;40&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>When Harry and Hermione lured Umbridge into the Forbidden Forest, Neville, Ron, Ginny, and Luna stayed alone with the Inquisitorial Squad. Neville and others broke free using skills that they had acquired in their D.A. sessions; Neville used good <a href="/wiki/Impediment_Jinx" title="Impediment Jinx">Impediment Jinx</a>. They then regrouped with Harry and Hermione, who had left Umbridge with a group of enraged centaurs. He, Ron, Ginny and Luna joined Harry and Hermione, who had left Umbridge at the grace of infuriated centaurs. They fly via <a href="/wiki/Thestral" title="Thestral">Thestrals</a> to London, despite Harry's reluctance to let them accompany him.<sup id="cite_ref-OP33_41-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-OP33-41">&#91;41&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 247px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/7/71/Neville_threatening_Bellatrix_GIF.gif/revision/latest?cb=20140425151948" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="245" height="125" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Neville threatening Bellatrix GIF.gif" data-image-key="Neville_threatening_Bellatrix_GIF.gif" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/7/71/Neville_threatening_Bellatrix_GIF.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/245?cb=20140425151948" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/7/71/Neville_threatening_Bellatrix_GIF.gif/revision/latest?cb=20140425151948" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/7/71/Neville_threatening_Bellatrix_GIF.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/245?cb=20140425151948" decoding="async" width="245" height="125" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Neville threatening Bellatrix GIF.gif" data-image-key="Neville_threatening_Bellatrix_GIF.gif" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/7/71/Neville_threatening_Bellatrix_GIF.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/245?cb=20140425151948" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Neville_threatening_Bellatrix_GIF.gif" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Neville meets Bellatrix Lestrange face-to-face in the Hall of Prophecy</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Once in the <a href="/wiki/Hall_of_Prophecy" title="Hall of Prophecy">Hall of Prophecies</a>, Harry was drawn to an orb that had his name on it. Neville and Hermione urged him not to remove it; once Harry had, the group was confronted by Death Eaters.<sup id="cite_ref-OP34_42-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-OP34-42">&#91;42&#93;</a></sup> In the subsequent battle, Neville accompanied Harry and Hermione. They run into the <a href="/wiki/Time_Room" title="Time Room">Time Room</a>, where he disarmed <a href="/wiki/Rabastan_Lestrange" title="Rabastan Lestrange">Rabastan Lestrange</a> who was struggling with Harry, accidentally disarming Harry as well. Wanting to fix his mistake he tried to stun Lestrange, but he hit a rack full of <a href="/wiki/Time-Turner" title="Time-Turner">time-turners</a>. Escaping from room he was hit by <a href="/wiki/Impediment_Jinx" title="Impediment Jinx">Impediment Jinx</a> by <a href="/wiki/Antonin_Dolohov" title="Antonin Dolohov">Antonin Dolohov</a> and <a href="/wiki/Jugson" title="Jugson">Jugson</a>, same as Harry and Hermione. When Hermione casted <a href="/wiki/Silencing_Charm" title="Silencing Charm">Silencing Charm</a> on Dolohov and Harry placed Jugson under <a href="/wiki/Full_Body-Bind_Curse" title="Full Body-Bind Curse">Full Body-Bind</a>, Dolohov cursed Hermione. Taking advantage of the moment Neville crawled from under the desk, but Dolohov broke Neville's nose and wand, so Harry placed Dolohov under Full Body-Bind. Neville refused Harry's suggestion that he leave with an incapacitated Hermione to go get help, instead carrying her while he and Harry searched for Ron, Ginny, and Luna. When several Death Eaters cornered Harry alone in the <a href="/wiki/Death_Chamber" title="Death Chamber">Death Chamber</a>, Neville stormed into the room to aid him, armed with Hermione's wand, but due to his broken nose, was unable to pronounce spells correctly.<sup id="cite_ref-OP35_43-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-OP35-43">&#91;43&#93;</a></sup> 
</p>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 252px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/4/45/Order-of-the-phoenix_neville_bellatrix.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20170528054404" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="250" height="103" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Order-of-the-phoenix neville bellatrix.jpg" data-image-key="Order-of-the-phoenix_neville_bellatrix.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/4/45/Order-of-the-phoenix_neville_bellatrix.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20170528054404" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/4/45/Order-of-the-phoenix_neville_bellatrix.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20170528054404" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/4/45/Order-of-the-phoenix_neville_bellatrix.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20170528054404" decoding="async" width="250" height="103" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Order-of-the-phoenix neville bellatrix.jpg" data-image-key="Order-of-the-phoenix_neville_bellatrix.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/4/45/Order-of-the-phoenix_neville_bellatrix.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20170528054404" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Order-of-the-phoenix_neville_bellatrix.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption"><a href="/wiki/Bellatrix_Lestrange" title="Bellatrix Lestrange">Bellatrix Lestrange</a> threatens Neville during the Battle of the Department of Mysteries</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>When another Death Eater seized Neville, Bellatrix Lestrange briefly tortured Neville with the <a href="/wiki/Cruciatus_Curse" title="Cruciatus Curse">Cruciatus Curse</a>, both to try to make Harry hand over <a href="/wiki/Sybill_Trelawney%27s_first_prophecy" title="Sybill Trelawney&#39;s first prophecy">the prophecy</a> and to see how long Neville held out before "cracking" like his parents. Even under the threat of being tortured (possibly even going insane like his parents), Neville told Harry not to hand the prophecy over.<sup id="cite_ref-OP35_43-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-OP35-43">&#91;43&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>After the <a href="/wiki/Order_of_the_Phoenix" title="Order of the Phoenix">Order of the Phoenix</a> members arrived, Harry tried to get out with Neville, but Harry was stopped by <a href="/wiki/Walden_Macnair" title="Walden Macnair">Walden Macnair</a>. Harry urged Neville to run, but Neville refused, instead breaking Macnair's grip on Harry by jabbing the Death Eater in the eye with Hermione's wand. Then Neville was strucked with <a href="/wiki/Dancing_Feet_Spell" title="Dancing Feet Spell">Dancing Feet Spell</a> by Dolohov, but Harry placed Dolohov under Body-Bind.<sup id="cite_ref-OP36_44-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-OP36-44">&#91;44&#93;</a></sup> Moments later they were attacked by <a href="/wiki/Lucius_Malfoy" title="Lucius Malfoy">Lucius Malfoy</a>. Harry throw Neville the prophecy to cast Impediment Jinx on Malfoy. As Harry pulled Neville up a flight of stairs, Neville accidentally smashed the prophecy. As the battle continued, Neville alerted Harry to the appearance of <a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore" title="Albus Dumbledore">Albus Dumbledore</a>. The battle soon ended, and Neville and his friends were transported back to Hogwarts, where Neville's nose was fixed by <a href="/wiki/Poppy_Pomfrey" title="Poppy Pomfrey">Poppy Pomfrey</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-OP38_45-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-OP38-45">&#91;45&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Harry soon learned the contents of the prophecy from Dumbledore. As both Neville and Harry were born at the close of <a href="/wiki/July" title="July">July</a> to parents who had all escaped Voldemort three times, they both qualified for the prophecy child.
