However, Dumbledore believed that the prophecy did indeed refer to Harry, not Neville, as <a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle" title="Tom Riddle">Voldemort</a> marked Harry as his equal by attacking him.<sup id="cite_ref-ootp37_2-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-ootp37-2">&#91;2&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Neville's grandmother purchased him a new wand, 13" cherry wood, with a unicorn hair core, from <a href="/wiki/Garrick_Ollivander" title="Garrick Ollivander">Garrick Ollivander</a> before his sixth year.
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Sixth_year">Sixth year</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Neville_Longbottom?veaction=edit&amp;section=9" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Sixth year">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Neville_Longbottom?action=edit&amp;section=9" title="Edit section: Sixth year"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry insists that Neville and Luna are cool friends"><b>Luna Lovegood</b>: "<i>People expect you to have cooler friends than us.</i>"</span></dd>
<dd><b>Harry Potter</b>: "<i>You </i>are<i> cool. None of them were at the Ministry. They didn’t <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_the_Department_of_Mysteries" title="Battle of the Department of Mysteries">fight with me</a>.</i>"</dd>
<dd><b>Luna Lovegood</b>: "<i>That’s a very nice thing to say.</i>"</dd>
<dd><b>Neville Longbottom</b>: "<i>We didn’t face him, though. You did. You should hear my gran talk about you. ‘That Harry Potter’s got more backbone than the whole Ministry of Magic put together!’ She’d give anything to have you as a grandson...</i>"</dd>
<dd>&#8212; Harry insists that Neville and Luna are cool friends<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Half-Blood_Prince" title="Harry Potter and the Half-Blood Prince">[src]</a></sup></dd></dl>
</div>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 252px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/f/f7/Neville_waiter_at_the_Slug_Club_Party.JPG/revision/latest?cb=20161121204533" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="250" height="111" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Neville waiter at the Slug Club Party.JPG" data-image-key="Neville_waiter_at_the_Slug_Club_Party.JPG" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/f/f7/Neville_waiter_at_the_Slug_Club_Party.JPG/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20161121204533" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/f/f7/Neville_waiter_at_the_Slug_Club_Party.JPG/revision/latest?cb=20161121204533" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/f/f7/Neville_waiter_at_the_Slug_Club_Party.JPG/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20161121204533" decoding="async" width="250" height="111" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Neville waiter at the Slug Club Party.JPG" data-image-key="Neville_waiter_at_the_Slug_Club_Party.JPG" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/f/f7/Neville_waiter_at_the_Slug_Club_Party.JPG/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20161121204533" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Neville_waiter_at_the_Slug_Club_Party.JPG" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Neville acting as a server during the <a href="/wiki/Slug_Club_Christmas_party" title="Slug Club Christmas party">Slug Club Christmas party</a></p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>On 1 September, 1996, Neville sat with <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter" title="Harry Potter">Harry Potter</a> and <a href="/wiki/Luna_Lovegood" title="Luna Lovegood">Luna Lovegood</a> on the Hogwarts Express, where both of them expressed disappointment that Harry did not plan to continue D.A. meetings during their sixth year. When <a href="/wiki/Romilda_Vane" title="Romilda Vane">Romilda Vane</a>, a younger <a href="/wiki/Gryffindor" title="Gryffindor">Gryffindor</a> student, invited Harry to come to her compartment and implicitly insulted Neville and Luna, Harry coldly rebuffed her, emphasising that Neville and Luna were among his closest and most loyal friends. Neville was later invited to join <a href="/wiki/Horace_Slughorn" title="Horace Slughorn">Horace Slughorn</a>, the new Potions professor, in his train compartment.<sup id="cite_ref-HBP7_46-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-HBP7-46">&#91;46&#93;</a></sup> Slughorn was searching for new students to add to his <a href="/wiki/Slug_Club" title="Slug Club">Slug Club</a>, but Neville didn't seem to meet Slughorn's requirements, and was not invited back to any of Slughorn's parties, but he was a server at Slughorn's Christmas party.
</p><p>Neville also achieved four known O.W.L.s: one '<a href="/wiki/Outstanding" title="Outstanding">Outstanding</a>', two '<a href="/wiki/Exceeds_Expectations" title="Exceeds Expectations">Exceeds Expectations</a>', and one '<a href="/wiki/Acceptable" title="Acceptable">Acceptable</a>'. The classes he were cleared to take were <a href="/wiki/Herbology" title="Herbology">Herbology</a>, <a href="/wiki/Charm" title="Charm">Charms</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Defence_Against_the_Dark_Arts" title="Defence Against the Dark Arts">Defence Against the Dark Arts</a>. The 'Acceptable' he achieved in <a href="/wiki/Transfiguration" title="Transfiguration">Transfiguration</a> was not good enough for <a href="/wiki/Nastily_Exhausting_Wizarding_Test" title="Nastily Exhausting Wizarding Test">N.E.W.T.</a>-level and he would not be able to keep up with the course work. McGonagall also stated that Professor Sprout will be delighted to see Neville back with an 'Outstanding' Herbology O.W.L.. He only applied for Transfiguration for his grandmother's desires, but McGonagall states it is time for Augusta to be proud of the grandson she has, as opposed to the one she desires. She let him down gently on his application on Transfiguration, and instead encouraged him to take Charms.
</p>
<dl><dd><div class="noprint"><i>Main article&#58; <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_the_Astronomy_Tower" title="Battle of the Astronomy Tower">Battle of the Astronomy Tower</a></i></div></dd></dl>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 252px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/0/06/B6C30M1_funeral_of_Albus_Dumbledore.png/revision/latest?cb=20161209004341" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="250" height="98" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="B6C30M1 funeral of Albus Dumbledore.png" data-image-key="B6C30M1_funeral_of_Albus_Dumbledore.png" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/0/06/B6C30M1_funeral_of_Albus_Dumbledore.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20161209004341" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/0/06/B6C30M1_funeral_of_Albus_Dumbledore.png/revision/latest?cb=20161209004341" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/0/06/B6C30M1_funeral_of_Albus_Dumbledore.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20161209004341" decoding="async" width="250" height="98" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="B6C30M1 funeral of Albus Dumbledore.png" data-image-key="B6C30M1_funeral_of_Albus_Dumbledore.png" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/0/06/B6C30M1_funeral_of_Albus_Dumbledore.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20161209004341" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:B6C30M1_funeral_of_Albus_Dumbledore.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">The funeral of Albus Dumbledore</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Towards the end of the school year, Neville participated in the Battle of the Astronomy Tower. Along with Luna Lovegood, he was the only member of <a href="/wiki/Dumbledore%27s_Army" title="Dumbledore&#39;s Army">Dumbledore's Army</a> to reply to the summons via the coins. Neville stood guard outside the <a href="/wiki/Room_of_Requirement" title="Room of Requirement">Room of Requirement</a> with Ron and Ginny, waiting for <a href="/wiki/Draco_Malfoy" title="Draco Malfoy">Draco Malfoy</a>, who evaded them by using <a href="/wiki/Peruvian_Instant_Darkness_Powder" title="Peruvian Instant Darkness Powder">Peruvian Instant Darkness Powder</a>. Neville suffered an injury that kept him in the hospital wing for some time, though he was able to attend the funeral of <a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore" title="Albus Dumbledore">Albus Dumbledore</a> shortly afterwards, where Luna helped him into his seat.<sup id="cite_ref-HBP30_47-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-HBP30-47">&#91;47&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Seventh_year">Seventh year</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Neville_Longbottom?veaction=edit&amp;section=10" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Seventh year">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Neville_Longbottom?action=edit&amp;section=10" title="Edit section: Seventh year"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows">"<i>Alecto, Amycus’s sister, teaches <a href="/wiki/Muggle_Studies" title="Muggle Studies">Muggle Studies</a>, which is compulsory for everyone. We’ve all got to listen to her explain how Muggles are like animals, stupid and dirty, and how they drive wizards into hiding by being vicious toward them, and how the natural order is being reestablished. I got this one ((indicates to a large gash on his cheek)) for asking her how much Muggle blood she and her brother have got.</i>"</span></dd>
<dd>&#8212;Neville explains Hogwarts new regime and his stand against the Carrows<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Deathly_Hallows" title="Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows">[src]</a></sup></dd>
<dd></dd></dl></div>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 252px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/f/f1/Neville_on_hogwarts_express.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20191205004714" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="250" height="104" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Neville on hogwarts express.jpg" data-image-key="Neville_on_hogwarts_express.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/f/f1/Neville_on_hogwarts_express.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20191205004714" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/f/f1/Neville_on_hogwarts_express.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20191205004714" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/f/f1/Neville_on_hogwarts_express.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20191205004714" decoding="async" width="250" height="104" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Neville on hogwarts express.jpg" data-image-key="Neville_on_hogwarts_express.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/f/f1/Neville_on_hogwarts_express.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20191205004714" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Neville_on_hogwarts_express.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Neville scorns Death Eaters searching for Harry Potter on the Hogwarts Express</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>On 1 August, 1997 <a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle" title="Tom Riddle">Lord Voldemort</a> took over the <a href="/wiki/British_Ministry_of_Magic" title="British Ministry of Magic">Ministry of Magic</a>. While <a href="/wiki/Muggle-borns" class="mw-redirect" title="Muggle-borns">Muggle-borns</a> were rounded up and Harry, Ron, and Hermione went on the run to search for Voldemort's <a href="/wiki/Horcrux" title="Horcrux">Horcruxes</a>, Neville returned to <a href="/wiki/Hogwarts_School_of_Witchcraft_and_Wizardry" title="Hogwarts School of Witchcraft and Wizardry">Hogwarts</a>, and, along with Ginny and Luna, restarted <a href="/wiki/Dumbledore%27s_Army" title="Dumbledore&#39;s Army">Dumbledore's Army</a>. The D.A. opposed the new headmaster, <a href="/wiki/Severus_Snape" title="Severus Snape">Severus Snape</a>, and the two new Death Eater professors, Alecto and <a href="/wiki/Amycus_Carrow" title="Amycus Carrow">Amycus Carrow</a>, who taught anti-<a href="/wiki/Non-magic_people" title="Non-magic people">Muggle</a> propaganda and the <a href="/wiki/Dark_Arts" title="Dark Arts">Dark Arts</a>. Neville got in trouble with the Carrows for refusing to practise the <a href="/wiki/Cruciatus_Curse" title="Cruciatus Curse">Cruciatus Curse</a> on other students as a method of punishment, as well as for standing up against their bigotry and cruelty.
</p>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 252px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/b/b5/Neville_battered.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20180205194943" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="250" height="248" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Neville battered.jpg" data-image-key="Neville_battered.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/b/b5/Neville_battered.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20180205194943" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/b/b5/Neville_battered.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20180205194943" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/b/b5/Neville_battered.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20180205194943" decoding="async" width="250" height="248" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Neville battered.jpg" data-image-key="Neville_battered.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/b/b5/Neville_battered.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20180205194943" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Neville_battered.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">A battered Neville, after being brutally punished by the Carrows</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure><p>The revived D.A. helped protect fellow students from being bullied by the <a href="/wiki/Death_Eaters" title="Death Eaters">Death Eater</a> teachers, and generally rebelled against authority, such as writing "<i>Dumbledore’s Army, still recruiting</i>" on the Hogwarts walls and freeing students from detention. Neville, Luna and Ginny also attempted to steal <a href="/wiki/Godric_Gryffindor%27s_Sword" class="mw-redirect" title="Godric Gryffindor&#39;s Sword">Godric Gryffindor's sword</a> from Snape's office, but were caught on the way out. In his own way to subvert the Carrows' manner of discipline, Snape only gave them a detention, sending them into the <a href="/wiki/Forbidden_Forest" title="Forbidden Forest">Forbidden Forest</a> with <a href="/wiki/Rubeus_Hagrid" title="Rubeus Hagrid">Hagrid</a>. Neville eventually decided to cease their open rebellion after <a href="/wiki/Michael_Corner" title="Michael Corner">Michael Corner</a> was caught and brutally tortured for freeing a chained-up first year.
</p><p>Neville was eventually left alone to lead the rebellion efforts, as Luna was dragged off the <a href="/wiki/Hogwarts_Express" title="Hogwarts Express">Hogwarts Express</a> by Death Eaters around Christmas of 1997 to coerce her father into ceasing his political dissidence in <i><a href="/wiki/The_Quibbler" title="The Quibbler">The Quibbler</a></i>, and Ginny did not return to Hogwarts following the Easter holidays, as her family went into hiding following Harry, Ron, and Hermione's <a href="/wiki/Skirmish_at_Malfoy_Manor" title="Skirmish at Malfoy Manor">escape from Malfoy Manor</a>. By this time, the Carrows were aware of Neville's role in the rebellion, and he suffered beatings and torture. The <a href="/wiki/British_Ministry_of_Magic" title="British Ministry of Magic">Ministry</a> also targeted Neville's grandmother to try to intimidate him, but she evaded capture and went on the run.
</p><p>Eventually, the Carrows realised that Neville was the main ringleader and decided that Hogwarts could do without him. Fearing that they may kill him, Neville made for the <a href="/wiki/Room_of_Requirement" title="Room of Requirement">Room of Requirement</a>, which he was able to turn into a hiding place for the D.A., and to connect to the <a href="/wiki/Hog%27s_Head" class="mw-redirect" title="Hog&#39;s Head">Hog's Head</a> in order to get food from <a href="/wiki/Aberforth_Dumbledore" title="Aberforth Dumbledore">Aberforth Dumbledore</a>. By May, most of the D.A. had taken to living there.<sup id="cite_ref-DH29_48-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-DH29-48">&#91;48&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Battle_of_Hogwarts"><a href="/wiki/Battle_of_Hogwarts" title="Battle of Hogwarts">Battle of Hogwarts</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Neville_Longbottom?veaction=edit&amp;section=11" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Battle of Hogwarts">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Neville_Longbottom?action=edit&amp;section=11" title="Edit section: Battle of Hogwarts"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows">"<i>The thing is, it helps when people stand up to them, it gives everyone hope. I used to notice that when you did it, Harry.</i>"</span></dd>
<dd>&#8212;Neville discussing the resistance to the Carrows at Hogwarts<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Deathly_Hallows" title="Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows">[src]</a></sup></dd>
<dd></dd></dl></div>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 252px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/e/ea/Trio_in_hogsmeade.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20160905203151" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="250" height="118" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Trio in hogsmeade.jpg" data-image-key="Trio_in_hogsmeade.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/e/ea/Trio_in_hogsmeade.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20160905203151" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/e/ea/Trio_in_hogsmeade.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20160905203151" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/e/ea/Trio_in_hogsmeade.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20160905203151" decoding="async" width="250" height="118" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Trio in hogsmeade.jpg" data-image-key="Trio_in_hogsmeade.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/e/ea/Trio_in_hogsmeade.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20160905203151" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Trio_in_hogsmeade.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">The trio and Neville in the <a href="/wiki/Hog%27s_Head_Inn" title="Hog&#39;s Head Inn">Hog's Head Inn</a></p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>On <a href="/wiki/2_May" title="2 May">2 May</a>, <a href="/wiki/1998" title="1998">1998</a> Neville enthusiastically greeted <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter" title="Harry Potter">Harry</a>, <a href="/wiki/Hermione_Granger" title="Hermione Granger">Hermione</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Ronald_Weasley" title="Ronald Weasley">Ron</a>, and led them from the Hog's Head into the <a href="/wiki/Room_of_Requirement" title="Room of Requirement">Room of Requirement</a>. While in the tunnel he explained to the trio the nature of his injuries and the reign of the Carrows at Hogwarts. He also informed the trio that the D.A. had been reinstated and was currently resisting the new regime. Believing that their return meant the overthrow of the <a href="/wiki/Death_Eaters" title="Death Eaters">Death Eater</a> professors, Neville signalled the rest of the D.A. to return to Hogwarts.<sup id="cite_ref-DH30_49-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-DH30-49">&#91;49&#93;</a></sup> As students returned, along with the <a href="/wiki/Order_of_the_Phoenix" title="Order of the Phoenix">Order of the Phoenix</a>, Voldemort and his Death Eater army approached, laying siege to the school in the hopes of capturing Harry Potter.<sup id="cite_ref-DH31_50-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-DH31-50">&#91;50&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows">"<i>Neville, who had emerged from nowhere brandishing armfuls of <a href="/wiki/Venomous_Tentacula" title="Venomous Tentacula">Venomous Tentacula</a>, which looped itself happily around the nearest Death Eater and began reeling him in.</i>"</span></dd>
<dd>&#8212;Neville fighting against the Death Eaters<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Deathly_Hallows" title="Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows">[src]</a></sup></dd>
<dd></dd></dl></div>
<p>During the first round of battle, Neville used various plants to attack Death Eaters, and helped transport the injured and dead when a temporary cease-fire was called. He briefly spoke to Harry, who told him that it was top priority to kill <a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle" title="Tom Riddle">Voldemort</a>'s <a href="/wiki/Snake" title="Snake">snake</a> and <a href="/wiki/Horcrux" title="Horcrux">Horcrux</a>, <a href="/wiki/Nagini" title="Nagini">Nagini</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-DH34_51-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-DH34-51">&#91;51&#93;</a></sup> When the Death Eaters approached with a "dead" Harry, Neville stood up in defiance of Voldemort. He was subsequently forced to wear the <a href="/wiki/Sorting_Hat" title="Sorting Hat">Sorting Hat</a> as it <a href="/wiki/Fire-Making_Spell" title="Fire-Making Spell">burned</a> because he refused to join Voldemort. Fortunately, due to Harry's sacrifice, Neville was able to shrug off the <a href="/wiki/Full_Body-Bind_Curse" title="Full Body-Bind Curse">Full Body-Bind Curse</a> with relative ease.<sup id="cite_ref-DH36_52-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-DH36-52">&#91;52&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 222px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/5/5f/Neville_kills_Nagini.gif/revision/latest?cb=20190821172011" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="220" height="92" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Neville kills Nagini.gif" data-image-key="Neville_kills_Nagini.gif" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/5/5f/Neville_kills_Nagini.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/220?cb=20190821172011" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/5/5f/Neville_kills_Nagini.gif/revision/latest?cb=20190821172011" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/5/5f/Neville_kills_Nagini.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/220?cb=20190821172011" decoding="async" width="220" height="92" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Neville kills Nagini.gif" data-image-key="Neville_kills_Nagini.gif" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/5/5f/Neville_kills_Nagini.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/220?cb=20190821172011" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Neville_kills_Nagini.gif" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Neville slaying <a href="/wiki/Nagini" title="Nagini">Nagini</a> with the Sword of Gryffindor</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Because of his tremendous bravery shown on the battlefield, Neville was able to pull <a href="/wiki/Godric_Gryffindor%27s_Sword" class="mw-redirect" title="Godric Gryffindor&#39;s Sword">Godric Gryffindor's sword</a> from the burning hat, in the process proving himself a true <a href="/wiki/Gryffindor" title="Gryffindor">Gryffindor</a>, something that was doubted constantly throughout due to his apparently weak-willed, shy, and bumbling nature. In a single stroke, he carried out Harry's final order, slaying Nagini, destroying Voldemort's last remaining <a href="/wiki/Horcrux" title="Horcrux">Horcrux</a>. Neville subsequently teamed up with <a href="/wiki/Ronald_Weasley" title="Ronald Weasley">Ron Weasley</a> as the defenders of Hogwarts and Death Eaters were forced into the <a href="/wiki/Great_Hall" title="Great Hall">Great Hall</a> and defeated <a href="/wiki/Fenrir_Greyback" title="Fenrir Greyback">Fenrir Greyback</a>. Also during the Battle Neville duelled <a href="/wiki/Scabior" title="Scabior">Scabior</a> on the Covered Bridge. Scabior fell to his death when the bridge fell down.<sup id="cite_ref-DH36_52-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-DH36-52">&#91;52&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Neville witnessed Harry's final defeat of Voldemort and survived the <a href="/wiki/Second_Wizarding_War" title="Second Wizarding War">Second Wizarding War</a>.
</p>
<h3><span id="Career_at_Hogwarts_(1998-2019)"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Career_at_Hogwarts_.281998-2019.29">Career at Hogwarts <span class="template-c">(1998-2019)</span></span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Neville_Longbottom?veaction=edit&amp;section=12" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Career at Hogwarts (1998-2019)">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Neville_Longbottom?action=edit&amp;section=12" title="Edit section: Career at Hogwarts (1998-2019)"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows"><b>Ginny Potter</b>: "<i>Don't forget to give Neville our love!</i>"</span></dd>
<dd><b>James Sirius</b>: "<i>Mum! I can't give a professor </i>love<i>...</i>"</dd>
<dd>&#8212; Ginny and her son exchange goodbyes at <a href="/wiki/Platform_Nine_and_Three-Quarters" title="Platform Nine and Three-Quarters">platform 9¾</a><sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Deathly_Hallows" title="Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows">[src]</a></sup></dd></dl>
</div>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 182px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/e/e1/Professor_Longbottom.png/revision/latest?cb=20200608002604" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="180" height="140" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Professor Longbottom.png" data-image-key="Professor_Longbottom.png" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/e/e1/Professor_Longbottom.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20200608002604" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/e/e1/Professor_Longbottom.png/revision/latest?cb=20200608002604" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/e/e1/Professor_Longbottom.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20200608002604" decoding="async" width="180" height="140" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Professor Longbottom.png" data-image-key="Professor_Longbottom.png" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/e/e1/Professor_Longbottom.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20200608002604" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Professor_Longbottom.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Neville Longbottom as a Hogwarts Professor</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Neville briefly worked as an <a href="/wiki/Auror" title="Auror">Auror</a>, immediately following the war.<sup id="cite_ref-PotterCast_53-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-PotterCast-53">&#91;53&#93;</a></sup> Sometime afterwards, he either sent an application to or was offered a place on the Hogwarts staff by <a href="/wiki/Headmaster" title="Headmaster">Headmistress</a> <a href="/wiki/Minerva_McGonagall" title="Minerva McGonagall">Minerva McGonagall</a>, and ultimately landed a teaching job in the <a href="/wiki/Herbology_department" title="Herbology department">Herbology department</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-DHEpilogue_4-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-DHEpilogue-4">&#91;4&#93;</a></sup> under <a href="/wiki/Head_of_Herbology" title="Head of Herbology">head of department</a>, <a href="/wiki/Pomona_Sprout" title="Pomona Sprout">Pomona Sprout</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-54" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-54">&#91;54&#93;</a></sup> Throughout his new career, his students would come to be impressed whenever he showed them his Dumbledore's Army coin, which he and other <a href="/wiki/Dumbledore%27s_Army" title="Dumbledore&#39;s Army">D.A.</a> members kept as a keepsake and had come to be seen as something of a badge of honour.<sup id="cite_ref-55" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-55">&#91;55&#93;</a></sup> Neville remained in contact with his old friends, as in <a href="/wiki/2017" title="2017">2017</a>, Ginny told her and Harry's <a href="/wiki/James_Potter_II" title="James Potter II">eldest son</a> "<i>to give Neville their love</i>" when he arrived at Hogwarts.<sup id="cite_ref-DHEpilogue_4-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-DHEpilogue-4">&#91;4&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Sometime before <a href="/wiki/2014" title="2014">2014</a>, he married his former classmate and D.A. member <a href="/wiki/Hannah_Abbott" title="Hannah Abbott">Hannah Abbott</a>. The pair lived at the <a href="/wiki/Leaky_Cauldron" title="Leaky Cauldron">Leaky Cauldron</a>, where she became the landlady.<sup id="cite_ref-hannah_56-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-hannah-56">&#91;56&#93;</a></sup> Hannah had retired from being landlady as of <a href="/wiki/2014" title="2014">2014</a>, she and Neville were childless and scathingly reported by <a href="/wiki/Rita_Skeeter" title="Rita Skeeter">Rita Skeeter</a> as "<i>enjoying a little more Ogden's Firewhisky than most would expect from custodians of our children</i>".<sup id="cite_ref-57" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-57">&#91;57&#93;</a></sup> Whether this is true or simply another scandalous rumour from Rita Skeeter is unknown. It was reported by Rita Skeeter that Neville is the godfather of Harry's second son, <a href="/wiki/Albus_Potter" title="Albus Potter">Albus Potter</a>.
</p><p>In <a href="/wiki/2019" title="2019">2019</a>, Neville aided members of the <a href="/wiki/Statute_of_Secrecy_Task_Force" title="Statute of Secrecy Task Force">Statute of Secrecy Task Force</a> who pursued a profession as a Professor by showing them a mental trick to make casting the <a href="/wiki/Deterioration_Hex" title="Deterioration Hex">Deterioration Hex</a> seem as a second nature to profoundly increase its effects, while he also instructed the Magizoologists how to use the <a href="/wiki/Bravery_Charm" title="Bravery Charm">Bravery Charm</a> to devastating effect.
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Physical_appearance">Physical appearance</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Neville_Longbottom?veaction=edit&amp;section=13" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Physical appearance">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Neville_Longbottom?action=edit&amp;section=13" title="Edit section: Physical appearance"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 182px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/b/b6/Neville_Longbottom.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20140610141612" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="180" height="280" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Neville Longbottom.jpg" data-image-key="Neville_Longbottom.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/b/b6/Neville_Longbottom.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20140610141612" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/b/b6/Neville_Longbottom.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20140610141612" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/b/b6/Neville_Longbottom.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20140610141612" decoding="async" width="180" height="280" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Neville Longbottom.jpg" data-image-key="Neville_Longbottom.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/b/b6/Neville_Longbottom.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20140610141612" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Neville_Longbottom.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Neville in his <a href="/wiki/Sixth_year" title="Sixth year">sixth year</a>, age 16</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Neville was said to strongly resemble <a href="/wiki/Alice_Longbottom" title="Alice Longbottom">his mother</a>. He was round-faced,<sup id="cite_ref-PS6_12-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-PS6-12">&#91;12&#93;</a></sup> short, chubby, and had blond hair.<sup id="cite_ref-58" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-58">&#91;58&#93;</a></sup> He was also somewhat buck-toothed. <a href="/wiki/Pansy_Parkinson" title="Pansy Parkinson">Pansy Parkinson</a> had once called him "<i>fat</i>", but this may have been an exaggeration, as she frequently made disparaging comments about Gryffindor students.<sup id="cite_ref-PS9_15-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-PS9-15">&#91;15&#93;</a></sup> 
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Personality_and_traits">Personality and traits</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Neville_Longbottom?veaction=edit&amp;section=14" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Personality and traits">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Neville_Longbottom?action=edit&amp;section=14" title="Edit section: Personality and traits"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Order of the Phoenix"><b>Bellatrix Lestrange </b>: "<i>Let's see how long Longbottom lasts before he cracks like his parents... unless <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter" title="Harry Potter">Potter</a> wants to give us the prophecy.</i>"</span></dd>
<dd><b>Neville</b>: "<i>DON'D GIB ID DO DEM! DON'D GIB ID DO DEM, HARRY!</i>"</dd>
<dd>&#8212; Neville defying Death Eaters with a broken nose<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Order_of_the_Phoenix" title="Harry Potter and the Order of the Phoenix">[src]</a></sup></dd></dl>
</div>
<p>When he was younger, Neville was clumsy, forgetful, shy, and many considered him ill-suited for <a href="/wiki/Gryffindor" title="Gryffindor">Gryffindor</a> house because he seemed timid. However, Neville proved that the <a href="/wiki/Sorting_Hat" title="Sorting Hat">Sorting Hat</a> had seen the bravery beneath his insecurity, as he stood up to his only friends as a first-year<sup id="cite_ref-PS6_12-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-PS6-12">&#91;12&#93;</a></sup> and later became one of the <a href="/wiki/Dumbledore%27s_Army" title="Dumbledore&#39;s Army">D.A.</a>’s most courageous members.<sup id="cite_ref-OP18_36-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-OP18-36">&#91;36&#93;</a></sup> Part of Neville’s problem seems to have been poor self-esteem, as he referred to himself as a "<i>nobody</i>" and "<i>almost a <a href="/wiki/Squib" title="Squib">Squib</a></i>"<sup id="cite_ref-CS11_22-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-CS11-22">&#91;22&#93;</a></sup> at times. This was likely caused by his grandmother’s belief that he was not living up to his parents’ accomplishments, and browbeating from fellow students and people like <a href="/wiki/Severus_Snape" title="Severus Snape">Professor Snape</a>. Though he came from a pure-blood family, he held no prejudice against <a href="/wiki/Half-blood" title="Half-blood">half-bloods</a> or <a href="/wiki/Muggle-born" title="Muggle-born">Muggle-borns</a>.
</p><p>Neville appeared to suffer from a degree of post-traumatic stress disorder, as the torture of a spider via the cruciatus curse by Barty Crouch Junior in disguise as <a href="/wiki/Alastor_Moody" title="Alastor Moody">Alastor Moody</a> was enough to cause him a severe anxiety attack. This was likely due to his own experience with his parents being subjected to the curse's worst possible outcome: the onset of permanent and complete insanity. This familiarity of what the <a href="/wiki/Cruciatus_Curse" title="Cruciatus Curse">Cruciatus Curse</a> could do in skilled enough hands was more than enough to terrify him.
</p>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 252px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/f/f7/Neville_plant.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20180310041409" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="250" height="126" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Neville plant.jpg" data-image-key="Neville_plant.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/f/f7/Neville_plant.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20180310041409" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/f/f7/Neville_plant.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20180310041409" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/f/f7/Neville_plant.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20180310041409" decoding="async" width="250" height="126" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Neville plant.jpg" data-image-key="Neville_plant.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/f/f7/Neville_plant.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20180310041409" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Neville_plant.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Neville and his interest in Herbology</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>With the support of his friends, the encouragement of <a href="/wiki/Remus_Lupin" title="Remus Lupin">Professor Lupin</a> to face his fears, and the motivation of knowing his parents’ torturers were on the loose, Neville became braver, more self-assured, and dedicated to the fight against <a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle" title="Tom Riddle">Lord Voldemort</a> and his Death Eaters.<sup id="cite_ref-OP25_39-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-OP25-39">&#91;39&#93;</a></sup> This was proven by his participation in many battles and his revival of the D.A. in the face of threats and torture at the hands of the <a href="/wiki/Alecto_and_Amycus_Carrow" title="Alecto and Amycus Carrow">Carrows</a> in his seventh year, as well as his defiance of Voldemort himself during the <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_Hogwarts" title="Battle of Hogwarts">final battle</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-DH29_48-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-DH29-48">&#91;48&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Throughout the trials he face over his seven years at <a href="/wiki/Hogwarts_School_of_Witchcraft_and_Wizardry" title="Hogwarts School of Witchcraft and Wizardry">Hogwarts</a>, Neville blossomed from a timid, self-deprecating, and generally nervous student into a stalwart soldier possessed of an ironclad will, courage of outstanding merit, and a nobility of spirit, despite still having a comical and shy but at the same time courageous and fierce. In many ways, Neville's transformation allowed him to change from a scaredy-cat into a lordly lion, becoming a ferocious defender of his fellow students during Voldemort's reign. Suffice it to say, Neville's appointment to Gryffindor House was well-deserved.
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Magical_abilities_and_skills">Magical abilities and skills</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Neville_Longbottom?veaction=edit&amp;section=15" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Magical abilities and skills">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Neville_Longbottom?action=edit&amp;section=15" title="Edit section: Magical abilities and skills"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Goblet of Fire">"<i>Apparently, <a href="/wiki/Pomona_Sprout" title="Pomona Sprout">Professor Sprout</a> told Professor Moody I'm really good at Herbology.</i>"</span></dd>
<dd>&#8212;Neville's talent in Herbology<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Goblet_of_Fire" title="Harry Potter and the Goblet of Fire">[src]</a></sup></dd>
<dd></dd></dl></div>
<p>Neville was not an academically strong student in his early years, often requiring <a href="/wiki/Hermione_Granger" title="Hermione Granger">Hermione</a>'s help in class and with school-work. However (as confirmed by <a href="/wiki/Minerva_McGonagall" title="Minerva McGonagall">McGonagall</a>), part of this was likely caused by his use of another's wand, poor self-esteem, and anxiety caused by the incessant bullying from many of his peers and <a href="/wiki/Severus_Snape" title="Severus Snape">Snape</a>. When he found both courage and self-confidence in his later years, Neville's <a href="/wiki/Magic" title="Magic">magical</a> skills as a <a href="/wiki/Wizardkind" title="Wizardkind">wizard</a> grew and he proved to be a powerful wizard in his own right. 
</p>
<ul><li><b><a href="/wiki/Herbology" title="Herbology">Herbology</a></b>: As confirmed by Professor Sprout, who taught Herbology at Hogwarts, Neville was particularly gifted at Herbology, with him seemingly being on par with <a href="/wiki/Hermione_Granger" title="Hermione Granger">Hermione Granger</a> in this subject. In his first year, Neville's Herbology score was so good that it even compensated for his abysmal Potions grade, and he was the fastest worker in class: in <a href="/wiki/1996" title="1996">1996</a>, he was the first to extract a pod from a <a href="/wiki/Snargaluff" title="Snargaluff">Snargaluff</a> plant.<sup id="cite_ref-HBP11_59-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-HBP11-59">&#91;59&#93;</a></sup> He later scored an "<a href="/wiki/Outstanding" title="Outstanding">Outstanding</a>" on his <a href="/wiki/Ordinary_Wizarding_Level" title="Ordinary Wizarding Level">O.W.L.</a> exam,<sup id="cite_ref-HBP9_60-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-HBP9-60">&#91;60&#93;</a></sup> helped Professor Sprout with organising the defenses around Hogwarts with <a href="/wiki/Devil%27s_Snare" title="Devil&#39;s Snare">Devil's Snare</a>, employed <a href="/wiki/Mandrake" title="Mandrake">Mandrakes</a> into the <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_Hogwarts" title="Battle of Hogwarts">Battle of Hogwarts</a> to attack the <a href="/wiki/Death_Eaters" title="Death Eaters">Death Eaters</a>, and even worked as the Hogwarts Professor of this subject himself after the <a href="/wiki/Second_Wizarding_War" title="Second Wizarding War">Second Wizarding War</a>. Neville's skills in Herbology would later serve him well in his brief career as an <a href="/wiki/Auror" title="Auror">Auror</a>. Neville would improve his already considerable skills in the field to the extent that he was eventually hired on as the new Herbology professor at Hogwarts, succeeding his mentor, Pomona Sprout.</li></ul>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Order of the Phoenix">"<i>He was improving so fast it was quite unnerving</i>"</span></dd>
<dd>&#8212;<a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter" title="Harry Potter">Harry Potter</a> about Neville regarding the D.A.<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Order_of_the_Phoenix" title="Harry Potter and the Order of the Phoenix">[src]</a></sup></dd>
<dd></dd></dl></div>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 227px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/c/c3/Neville_Riddikulus.gif/revision/latest?cb=20190402102647" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="225" height="94" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Neville Riddikulus.gif" data-image-key="Neville_Riddikulus.gif" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/c/c3/Neville_Riddikulus.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/225?cb=20190402102647" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/c/c3/Neville_Riddikulus.gif/revision/latest?cb=20190402102647" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/c/c3/Neville_Riddikulus.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/225?cb=20190402102647" decoding="async" width="225" height="94" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Neville Riddikulus.gif" data-image-key="Neville_Riddikulus.gif" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/c/c3/Neville_Riddikulus.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/225?cb=20190402102647" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Neville_Riddikulus.gif" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Neville mastering the <a href="/wiki/Boggart-Banishing_Spell" title="Boggart-Banishing Spell">Boggart-Banishing Spell</a></p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<ul><li><b><a href="/wiki/Defence_Against_the_Dark_Arts" title="Defence Against the Dark Arts">Defence Against the Dark Arts</a></b>: Once properly motivated by <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter" title="Harry Potter">Harry Potter</a> during <a href="/wiki/Dumbledore%27s_Army" title="Dumbledore&#39;s Army">Dumbledore's Army</a> meeting, and made more confident, Neville proved to be proficient in Defence Against the Dark Arts. Indeed, Neville even achieved an '<a href="/wiki/Exceeds_Expectations" title="Exceeds Expectations">Exceeds Expectations</a>' on his O.W.L. exam, which allowed him to advance to <a href="/wiki/Nastily_Exhausting_Wizarding_Test" title="Nastily Exhausting Wizarding Test">N.E.W.T.</a>-level.<sup id="cite_ref-HBP9_60-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-HBP9-60">&#91;60&#93;</a></sup> Neville's talent with defensive spells and <a href="/wiki/Counter-curse" title="Counter-curse">Counter-curses</a> was also proven in the <a href="/wiki/Second_Wizarding_War" title="Second Wizarding War">Second Wizarding War</a> (which he survived), as well as his brief post-war work as an <a href="/wiki/Auror" title="Auror">Auror</a>.</li>
<li><b><a href="/wiki/Duelling" title="Duelling">Duelling</a></b>: Neville proved to be a surprisingly skilled and competent duellist after gaining the required confidence and motivation from his time in <a href="/wiki/Dumbledore%27s_Army" title="Dumbledore&#39;s Army">Dumbledore's Army</a>: he survived the <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_the_Department_of_Mysteries" title="Battle of the Department of Mysteries">Battle of the Department of Mysteries</a> without any serious injuries, and was notably the last person — apart from Harry Potter — standing until the <a href="/wiki/Order_of_the_Phoenix" title="Order of the Phoenix">Order of the Phoenix</a> arrived to rescue them. During the <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_Hogwarts" title="Battle of Hogwarts">Battle of Hogwarts</a><sup id="cite_ref-DH31_50-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-DH31-50">&#91;50&#93;</a></sup> he defeated <a href="/wiki/Fenrir_Greyback" title="Fenrir Greyback">Fenrir Greyback</a>, along with <a href="/wiki/Ronald_Weasley" title="Ronald Weasley">Ron</a> and was one of the survivors.<sup id="cite_ref-DH36_52-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-DH36-52">&#91;52&#93;</a></sup> It was also highly likely that, due to his hands-on experience from serving as <a href="/wiki/Auror" title="Auror">Auror</a>, Neville's skills in <a href="/wiki/Martial_magic" title="Martial magic">martial magic</a> later increased considerably even further.</li>
<li><b><a href="/wiki/Charm" title="Charm">Charms</a></b>: Neville proved to be highly talented in charm-work, earning an 'Exceeds Expectations' in the subject on his O.W.L. exam.<sup id="cite_ref-HBP9_60-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-HBP9-60">&#91;60&#93;</a></sup> Apart from Hermione, he mastered the <a href="/wiki/Shield_Charm" title="Shield Charm">Shield Charm</a> more quickly than anyone in <a href="/wiki/Dumbledore%27s_Army" title="Dumbledore&#39;s Army">Dumbledore's Army</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-OP25_39-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-OP25-39">&#91;39&#93;</a></sup> He could also effectively perform simpler charms, such as the <a href="/wiki/Locking_Spell" title="Locking Spell">Locking Spell</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-OP34_42-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-OP34-42">&#91;42&#93;</a></sup> and the <a href="/wiki/Banishing_Charm" title="Banishing Charm">Banishing Charm</a> (though his aim was initially imperfect with this spell). Neville could even produce a non-corporeal <a href="/wiki/Patronus_Charm" title="Patronus Charm">Patronus Charm</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-OP27_8-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-OP27-8">&#91;8&#93;</a></sup> proving of his superior magical ability given the immense difficulty required with casting such an advanced and powerful protective charm. It was likely that he eventually managed to produce a full, corporeal Patronus, and also improved his general Charms work during his work as an Auror.</li>
<li><b><a href="/wiki/Transfiguration" title="Transfiguration">Transfiguration</a></b>: Though not excellent in this subject, <a href="/wiki/Minerva_McGonagall" title="Minerva McGonagall">Professor McGonagall</a> stated that Neville's work only lacked confidence. With that said, Neville managed to score an '<a href="/wiki/Acceptable" title="Acceptable">Acceptable</a>' on his Transfiguration O.W.L., but he was unable to continue into the <a href="/wiki/Nastily_Exhausting_Wizarding_Test" title="Nastily Exhausting Wizarding Test">N.E.W.T.</a>-level.<sup id="cite_ref-HBP9_60-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-HBP9-60">&#91;60&#93;</a></sup> However, it was likely that Neville's skills in the subject improved to some extent after his serving as an Auror, given how Transfiguration is commonly used in the job, and therefore he would have had more experience using it.</li>
<li><b>Leadership skills</b>: During the <a href="/wiki/1997-1998_school_year" class="mw-redirect" title="1997-1998 school year">1997-1998 school year</a>, Neville co-led <a href="/wiki/Dumbledore%27s_Army" title="Dumbledore&#39;s Army">Dumbledore's Army</a> along side <a href="/wiki/Ginevra_Weasley" title="Ginevra Weasley">Ginny</a> and <a href="/wiki/Luna_Lovegood" title="Luna Lovegood">Luna</a>. His leadership proved to be so efficient, that the <a href="/wiki/Death_Eaters" title="Death Eaters">Death Eaters</a> were forced to resort to attempting to control Neville through his grandmother, and he was forced to go into hiding in the <a href="/wiki/Room_of_Requirement" title="Room of Requirement">Room of Requirement</a>. Neville's leadership skills would later aid him in his career as the <a href="/wiki/Herbology" title="Herbology">Herbology</a> professor at <a href="/wiki/Hogwarts_School_of_Witchcraft_and_Wizardry" title="Hogwarts School of Witchcraft and Wizardry">Hogwarts</a> in his later life.</li>
<li><b>Indomitable willpower</b>: As he got older and gained more courage and self-confidence, Neville was shown to have quite a strong willpower and unbreakable spirit in contrast to his earlier years when he often crumbled under the bullying from <a href="/wiki/Draco_Malfoy" title="Draco Malfoy">Draco Malfoy</a>, <a href="/wiki/Severus_Snape" title="Severus Snape">Severus Snape</a> and most of the Slytherin Students. This was first shown in the <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_the_Department_of_Mysteries" title="Battle of the Department of Mysteries">Battle of the Department of Mysteries</a> when he stood up to <a href="/wiki/Bellatrix_Lestrange" title="Bellatrix Lestrange">Bellatrix Lestrange</a> despite being tortured by her in response when she callously remarked that she had the pleasure of meeting and torturing both his parents, even though she was one of <a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle" title="Tom Riddle">Voldemort</a>'s most powerful and loyal <a href="/wiki/Death_Eaters" title="Death Eaters">Death Eaters</a> and was also the last person standing alongside Harry before the <a href="/wiki/Order_of_the_Phoenix" title="Order of the Phoenix">Order of the Phoenix</a> arrived to rescue them. He again showed his indomitable willpower when the Death Eaters took control of Hogwarts, standing up to the <a href="/wiki/Alecto_and_Amycus_Carrow" title="Alecto and Amycus Carrow">Carrow's</a> and Snape (unaware Snape was secretly still on their side) along with reforming <a href="/wiki/Dumbledore%27s_Army" title="Dumbledore&#39;s Army">Dumbledore's Army</a>, despite the torturous punishments he and many of the students received for opposing the Death Eater's regime. Neville later fought against the Death Eaters in the <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_Hogwarts" title="Battle of Hogwarts">Battle of Hogwarts</a> and stood up to Voldemort himself upon Harry's alleged death by refusing his offer to join him and the Death Eaters, showing how much he had transformed since his earlier years. His defiance of Voldemort allowed him to destroy Voldemort's last remaining <a href="/wiki/Horcrux" title="Horcrux">Horcrux</a> <a href="/wiki/Nagini" title="Nagini">Nagini</a> and also allowed Harry to defeat Voldemort for the final time.</li></ul>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Possessions">Possessions</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Neville_Longbottom?veaction=edit&amp;section=16" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Possessions">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Neville_Longbottom?action=edit&amp;section=16" title="Edit section: Possessions"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 202px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/f/f0/Neville%27s_wand.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20141209002728" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="200" height="200" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Neville&#39;s wand.jpg" data-image-key="Neville&#39;s_wand.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/f/f0/Neville%27s_wand.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/200?cb=20141209002728" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/f/f0/Neville%27s_wand.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20141209002728" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/f/f0/Neville%27s_wand.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/200?cb=20141209002728" decoding="async" width="200" height="200" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Neville&#39;s wand.jpg" data-image-key="Neville&#39;s_wand.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/f/f0/Neville%27s_wand.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/200?cb=20141209002728" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Neville%27s_wand.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Neville's second wand: 13", cherry wood, and unicorn hair core</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<ul><li><b><a href="/wiki/Neville_Longbottom%27s_first_wand" title="Neville Longbottom&#39;s first wand">First wand</a></b>: Neville's first wand was inherited from his father, Frank Longbottom. Its length, wood, and core material were unknown, and it was destroyed by <a href="/wiki/Antonin_Dolohov" title="Antonin Dolohov">Antonin Dolohov</a> during the <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_the_Department_of_Mysteries" title="Battle of the Department of Mysteries">Battle of the Department of Mysteries</a>.</li>
<li><b><a href="/wiki/Neville_Longbottom%27s_second_wand" title="Neville Longbottom&#39;s second wand">Second wand</a></b>: Neville's second wand was 13" long, made of <a href="/wiki/Cherry_(tree)" title="Cherry (tree)">cherry</a> <a href="/wiki/Wand_wood" title="Wand wood">wood</a>, and had a <a href="/wiki/Unicorn_hair" title="Unicorn hair">unicorn hair</a> <a href="/wiki/Wand_core" title="Wand core">core</a>. This wand was manufactured by <a href="/wiki/Garrick_Ollivander" title="Garrick Ollivander">Garrick Ollivander</a> sometime in or before <a href="/wiki/1996" title="1996">1996</a>, and purchased from his wand shop <a href="/wiki/Ollivanders" title="Ollivanders">Ollivanders</a> in <a href="/wiki/Diagon_Alley" title="Diagon Alley">Diagon Alley</a>.</li>
<li><b><a href="/wiki/Neville_Longbottom%27s_bedroom" title="Neville Longbottom&#39;s bedroom">Bedroom</a></b>: Neville's bedroom was located in Augusta Longbottom's house. Augusta once joked that he had been given enough wrappers by his mother to paper his bedroom.</li></ul>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 182px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/4/41/Trevor_PM.png/revision/latest?cb=20170117131957" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="180" height="177" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Trevor PM.png" data-image-key="Trevor_PM.png" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/4/41/Trevor_PM.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20170117131957" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/4/41/Trevor_PM.png/revision/latest?cb=20170117131957" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/4/41/Trevor_PM.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20170117131957" decoding="async" width="180" height="177" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Trevor PM.png" data-image-key="Trevor_PM.png" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/4/41/Trevor_PM.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20170117131957" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Trevor_PM.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Trevor, Neville's pet toad</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<ul><li><b><a href="/wiki/Trevor" title="Trevor">Trevor</a></b>: Trevor was Neville's pet <a href="/wiki/Toad" title="Toad">toad</a>. He was given to Neville by his Great-Uncle Algie upon Neville's gaining admission to Hogwarts School of Witchcraft and Wizardry.</li></ul>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 182px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/4/4f/Remembrall-neville.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20110821124033" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="180" height="173" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Remembrall-neville.jpg" data-image-key="Remembrall-neville.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/4/4f/Remembrall-neville.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20110821124033" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/4/4f/Remembrall-neville.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20110821124033" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/4/4f/Remembrall-neville.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20110821124033" decoding="async" width="180" height="173" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Remembrall-neville.jpg" data-image-key="Remembrall-neville.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/4/4f/Remembrall-neville.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20110821124033" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Remembrall-neville.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Neville's Remembrall</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<ul><li><b><a href="/wiki/Remembrall" title="Remembrall">Remembrall</a></b>: Neville was gifted one these <a href="/wiki/Magic" title="Magic">magical</a> items by his grandmother for the <a href="/wiki/1991%E2%80%931992_school_year" title="1991–1992 school year">1991–1992 school year</a>, in an attempt to help him remember things, to counter his frequent absent-mindedness. His Remembrall would turn red in colour whenever he forgot something; the only trouble being, he could often not remember what he had even forgotten.</li></ul>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 182px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/0/07/Mimblus.PNG/revision/latest?cb=20161217054950" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="180" height="255" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Mimblus.PNG" data-image-key="Mimblus.PNG" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/0/07/Mimblus.PNG/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20161217054950" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/0/07/Mimblus.PNG/revision/latest?cb=20161217054950" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/0/07/Mimblus.PNG/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20161217054950" decoding="async" width="180" height="255" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Mimblus.PNG" data-image-key="Mimblus.PNG" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/0/07/Mimblus.PNG/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20161217054950" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Mimblus.PNG" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Mimbulus Mimbletonia</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<ul><li><b><a href="/wiki/Mimbulus_mimbletonia" title="Mimbulus mimbletonia">Mimbulus mimbletonia</a></b>: Neville was gifted a pot of this very rare magical plant for his birthday before the start of the <a href="/wiki/1995%E2%80%931996_school_year" title="1995–1996 school year">1995–1996 school year</a>, due to his love and talent for <a href="/wiki/Herbology" title="Herbology">Herbology</a>. He was skilled in caring for this plant, and had knowledge of its species, including its <a href="/wiki/Stinksap" title="Stinksap">Stinksap</a>.</li>
<li><i><b><a href="/wiki/Magical_Mediterranean_Water-Plants_and_Their_Properties" title="Magical Mediterranean Water-Plants and Their Properties">Magical Mediterranean Water-Plants and Their Properties</a></b></i>: Neville was gifted a copy of this <a href="/wiki/Herbology" title="Herbology">Herbology</a> book by <a href="/wiki/Professor" title="Professor">Professor</a> <a href="/wiki/Bartemius_Crouch_Junior" title="Bartemius Crouch Junior">Bartemius Crouch Junior</a> (then disguised as <a href="/wiki/Alastor_Moody" title="Alastor Moody">Alastor Moody</a>) in <a href="/wiki/1994" title="1994">1994</a>, in an attempt for him to inform <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter" title="Harry Potter">Harry Potter</a> about <a href="/wiki/Gillyweed" title="Gillyweed">Gillyweed</a> for the <a href="/wiki/Triwizard_Tournament" title="Triwizard Tournament">Triwizard Tournament</a>.</li>
<li><i><b><a href="/wiki/Winogrand%27s_Wondrous_Water_Plants" title="Winogrand&#39;s Wondrous Water Plants">Winogrand's Wondrous Water Plants</a></b></i>: Neville owned a copy of this <a href="/wiki/Herbology" title="Herbology">Herbology</a> book, at least since <a href="/wiki/1994" title="1994">1994</a>, and kept it with him while hiding in the <a href="/wiki/Room_of_Requirement" title="Room of Requirement">Room of Requirement</a> in <a href="/wiki/1998" title="1998">1998</a> with <a href="/wiki/Dumbledore%27s_Army" title="Dumbledore&#39;s Army">Dumbledore's Army</a>.</li>
<li><b><a href="/wiki/Pointed_purple_crystal" title="Pointed purple crystal">Pointed purple crystal</a></b>: Neville purchased one of these supposedly protective items during the <a href="/wiki/1992%E2%80%931993_school_year" title="1992–1993 school year">1992–1993 school year</a>, when the <a href="/wiki/Chamber_of_Secrets" title="Chamber of Secrets">Chamber of Secrets</a> was <a href="/wiki/Plot_to_open_the_Chamber_of_Secrets" title="Plot to open the Chamber of Secrets">re-opened</a>, to protect himself from the "<a href="/wiki/Serpent_of_Slytherin" title="Serpent of Slytherin">monster</a>" within that was <a href="/wiki/Petrification" title="Petrification">attacking</a> <a href="/wiki/Muggle-born" title="Muggle-born">Muggle-born</a> students. It was most likely completely useless, and was very little utility to Neville, given his status as a <a href="/wiki/Pure-blood" title="Pure-blood">pure-blood</a>, and was thus highly unlikely to attack.</li></ul>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Relationships">Relationships</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Neville_Longbottom?veaction=edit&amp;section=17" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Relationships">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Neville_Longbottom?action=edit&amp;section=17" title="Edit section: Relationships"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Family">Family</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Neville_Longbottom?veaction=edit&amp;section=18" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Family">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Neville_Longbottom?action=edit&amp;section=18" title="Edit section: Family"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Parents">Parents</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Neville_Longbottom?veaction=edit&amp;section=19" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Parents">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Neville_Longbottom?action=edit&amp;section=19" title="Edit section: Parents"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Order of the Phoenix"><b>Augusta Longbottom</b>: "<i>What's this? Haven't you told your friends about your parents, Neville? Well, it’s nothing to be ashamed of! You should be proud, Neville, proud! They didn’t give their health and their sanity so their only son would be ashamed of them, you know!</i>"</span></dd>
<dd><b>Neville Longbottom</b>: "<i>I’m not ashamed.</i>"</dd>
<dd><b>Augusta Longbottom</b>: "<i>Well, you’ve got a funny way of showing it!</i>"</dd>
<dd>&#8212; Augusta telling Neville to be proud of his parents<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Order_of_the_Phoenix" title="Harry Potter and the Order of the Phoenix">[src]</a></sup></dd></dl>
</div><figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 334px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/7/76/Longbottom_family_portrait.png/revision/latest?cb=20170730190047" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="332" height="193" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Longbottom family portrait.png" data-image-key="Longbottom_family_portrait.png" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/7/76/Longbottom_family_portrait.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/332?cb=20170730190047" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/7/76/Longbottom_family_portrait.png/revision/latest?cb=20170730190047" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/7/76/Longbottom_family_portrait.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/332?cb=20170730190047" decoding="async" width="332" height="193" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Longbottom family portrait.png" data-image-key="Longbottom_family_portrait.png" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/7/76/Longbottom_family_portrait.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/332?cb=20170730190047" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Longbottom_family_portrait.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Frank and Alice with baby Neville</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>As Neville's parents, Alice and Frank Longbottom, had been permanent residents of <a href="/wiki/St_Mungo%27s_Hospital_for_Magical_Maladies_and_Injuries" title="St Mungo&#39;s Hospital for Magical Maladies and Injuries">St Mungo's Hospital for Magical Maladies and Injuries</a> since Neville's infancy, he never knew them as the popular and talented Aurors they were reputed to be. Nevertheless, he held them in high esteem, much like his friend Harry looked up to the parents he never knew.
</p><p>Neville regularly visited his parents at St Mungo's with his grandmother, where he tried to speak to them and brought them sweets, keeping the wrappers his mother handed back to him, even when his grandmother told him to throw them in the bin.<sup id="cite_ref-OP23_38-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-OP23-38">&#91;38&#93;</a></sup> Their torture clearly haunted him, as he was badly shaken by seeing the <a href="/wiki/Cruciatus_Curse" title="Cruciatus Curse">Cruciatus Curse</a> demonstrated on a spider in his <a href="/wiki/1994" title="1994">fourth year</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-GF14_30-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-GF14-30">&#91;30&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>When the Lestranges escaped from <a href="/wiki/Azkaban" title="Azkaban">Azkaban</a> in <a href="/wiki/1996" title="1996">1996</a>, Neville did not discuss it, but he became very dedicated to his training in <a href="/wiki/Dumbledore%27s_Army" title="Dumbledore&#39;s Army">Dumbledore's Army</a>. During the <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_the_Department_of_Mysteries" title="Battle of the Department of Mysteries">Battle of the Department of Mysteries</a>, he was taunted about his parents by <a href="/wiki/Bellatrix_Lestrange" title="Bellatrix Lestrange">Bellatrix Lestrange</a>, who also briefly subjected him to the Cruciatus Curse, but Neville remained defiant.<sup id="cite_ref-OP35_43-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-OP35-43">&#91;43&#93;</a></sup> Neville would later carry on their legacy as a resistance fighter against Voldemort's regime at Hogwarts, and later in his brief career as an Auror.
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Augusta_Longbottom">Augusta Longbottom</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Neville_Longbottom?veaction=edit&amp;section=20" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Augusta Longbottom">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Neville_Longbottom?action=edit&amp;section=20" title="Edit section: Augusta Longbottom"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 182px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/0/03/AugustaLongbottomPS.png/revision/latest?cb=20151229011507" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="180" height="240" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="AugustaLongbottomPS.png" data-image-key="AugustaLongbottomPS.png" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/0/03/AugustaLongbottomPS.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20151229011507" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/0/03/AugustaLongbottomPS.png/revision/latest?cb=20151229011507" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/0/03/AugustaLongbottomPS.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20151229011507" decoding="async" width="180" height="240" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="AugustaLongbottomPS.png" data-image-key="AugustaLongbottomPS.png" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/0/03/AugustaLongbottomPS.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20151229011507" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:AugustaLongbottomPS.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption"><a href="/wiki/Augusta_Longbottom" title="Augusta Longbottom">Augusta Longbottom</a>, his paternal grandmother</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows"><b>Augusta Longbottom</b>: "<i>Have you seen my grandson?</i>"</span></dd>
<dd><b>Harry Potter</b>: "<i>He’s fighting.</i>"</dd>
<dd><b>Augusta Longbottom</b>: "<i>Naturally. Excuse me, I must go and assist him.</i>"</dd>
<dd>&#8212; Augusta during the <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_Hogwarts" title="Battle of Hogwarts">Battle of Hogwarts</a><sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Deathly_Hallows" title="Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows">[src]</a></sup></dd></dl>
</div>
<p>Neville was raised by his grandmother, Augusta Longbottom, after his parents were <a href="/wiki/Cruciatus_Curse" title="Cruciatus Curse">tortured</a> to the point of insanity when he was an infant. This was pivotal in the development of his personality, as his grandmother often expressed her disappointment with her grandson's seeming lack of magical ability, and what she considered his inability to live up to his parents' skills. By Minerva McGonagall's claim, however, Augusta should be proud of the grandson she has, as opposed to the one she wants.
</p><p>When Neville was a child, his grandmother, as well as some of his other <a href="/wiki/Longbottom_family" title="Longbottom family">relatives</a>, feared that he might have been a <a href="/wiki/Squib" title="Squib">Squib</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-CS11_22-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-CS11-22">&#91;22&#93;</a></sup> However, when Neville showed great bravery and heroism during the <a href="/wiki/Second_Wizarding_War" title="Second Wizarding War">Second Wizarding War</a>, his grandmother was clearly very proud of him. She came to Hogwarts during the final battle and ran off to assist him in fighting <a href="/wiki/Death_Eaters" title="Death Eaters">Death Eaters</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-DH31_50-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-DH31-50">&#91;50&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Uncle_Algie">Uncle Algie</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Neville_Longbottom?veaction=edit&amp;section=21" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Uncle Algie">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Neville_Longbottom?action=edit&amp;section=21" title="Edit section: Uncle Algie"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>Neville appeared to be fairly close to his great-uncle <a href="/wiki/Algie_Longbottom" title="Algie Longbottom">Algie</a>, who tried to "scare" magic into him when he was younger; he once accidentally dropped Neville out of a window while reaching for a meringue, and when Neville bounced, his family was pleased to discover that he was not, in fact, a Squib. Algie later rewarded him with his pet toad <a href="/wiki/Trevor" title="Trevor">Trevor</a> for getting into Hogwarts. Algie and Neville appear to have shared an interest in <a href="/wiki/Herbology" title="Herbology">Herbology</a>, as Algie gave Neville his very rare <a href="/wiki/Mimbulus_mimbletonia" title="Mimbulus mimbletonia">Mimbulus mimbletonia</a> plant, which at one point was the password to the <a href="/wiki/Gryffindor_Tower" title="Gryffindor Tower">Gryffindor Common Room</a>.
