However, as Algie was willing to risk Neville's life to reveal his magic, such as pushing him into a lake and dangling him from a window, Algie more then likely cares for Neville's magic more than the boy himself.
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Hannah_Abbott">Hannah Abbott</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Neville_Longbottom?veaction=edit&amp;section=22" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Hannah Abbott">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Neville_Longbottom?action=edit&amp;section=22" title="Edit section: Hannah Abbott"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 176px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/3/33/Abbot_cropped.PNG/revision/latest?cb=20100103014122" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="174" height="272" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Abbot cropped.PNG" data-image-key="Abbot_cropped.PNG" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/3/33/Abbot_cropped.PNG/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/174?cb=20100103014122" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/3/33/Abbot_cropped.PNG/revision/latest?cb=20100103014122" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/3/33/Abbot_cropped.PNG/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/174?cb=20100103014122" decoding="async" width="174" height="272" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Abbot cropped.PNG" data-image-key="Abbot_cropped.PNG" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/3/33/Abbot_cropped.PNG/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/174?cb=20100103014122" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Abbot_cropped.PNG" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption"><a href="/wiki/Hannah_Abbott" title="Hannah Abbott">Hannah Abbott</a>, his future wife</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Neville and <a href="/wiki/Hannah_Abbott" title="Hannah Abbott">Hannah Abbott</a> were never shown as being more than classmates during school. Since Hannah was in <a href="/wiki/Hufflepuff" title="Hufflepuff">Hufflepuff House</a> and Neville in <a href="/wiki/Gryffindor" title="Gryffindor">Gryffindor</a>, they probably did not spend too much time together, though it is possible that they became friends when they were both members of <a href="/wiki/Dumbledore%27s_Army" title="Dumbledore&#39;s Army">Dumbledore's Army</a>. Sometime after leaving Hogwarts, Neville and Hannah married and moved into the <a href="/wiki/Leaky_Cauldron" title="Leaky Cauldron">Leaky Cauldron</a>, where she worked as the landlady and Neville as the Hogwarts Herbology teacher.
</p><p>It is also possible that she and Neville became close during Herbology lessons, as those were shared by <a href="/wiki/Gryffindor" title="Gryffindor">Gryffindor</a> and <a href="/wiki/Hufflepuff" title="Hufflepuff">Hufflepuff</a> of their year. It stands to reason that, since Herbology was where Neville excelled, he may have been confident and even charming amongst the plant life, thus attracting Hannah's attention. Since Hannah lost her mother in her sixth year, it may also have been Neville's ability to sympathise with her grief that brought the two together, or simply Hannah felt attracted to Neville's heroism in the Battle of Hogwarts and when the war was over she kept contact with him, they fell in love and got married.
</p><p>Hannah is eventually retrained as a Healer and applies to become the new matron of Hogwarts, a job held by <a href="/wiki/Poppy_Pomfrey" title="Poppy Pomfrey">Poppy Pomfrey</a> during their years as students. It is possible that she applied in order to be closer to Neville. However, in the year 2020, Madame Pomfrey is seen to still be the matron, as she resets <a href="/wiki/Albus_Potter" title="Albus Potter">Albus Potter</a>'s broken arm.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Trevor">Trevor</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Neville_Longbottom?veaction=edit&amp;section=23" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Trevor">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Neville_Longbottom?action=edit&amp;section=23" title="Edit section: Trevor"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 252px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/5/5a/Trevor.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20180606134505" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="250" height="104" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Trevor.jpg" data-image-key="Trevor.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/5/5a/Trevor.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20180606134505" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/5/5a/Trevor.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20180606134505" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/5/5a/Trevor.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20180606134505" decoding="async" width="250" height="104" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Trevor.jpg" data-image-key="Trevor.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/5/5a/Trevor.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20180606134505" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Trevor.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption"><a href="/wiki/Trevor" title="Trevor">Trevor</a>, his pet <a href="/wiki/Toad" title="Toad">toad</a></p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Trevor was Neville's pet toad. He was given to Neville by his Uncle <a href="/wiki/Algie_Longbottom" title="Algie Longbottom">Algie</a> upon Neville's gaining admission to <a href="/wiki/Hogwarts_School_of_Witchcraft_and_Wizardry" title="Hogwarts School of Witchcraft and Wizardry">Hogwarts School of Witchcraft and Wizardry</a>. Neville often lost Trevor, as he did the first time he rode the <a href="/wiki/Hogwarts_Express" title="Hogwarts Express">Hogwarts Express</a> and <a href="/wiki/Hermione_Granger" title="Hermione Granger">Hermione Granger</a> met <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter" title="Harry Potter">Harry Potter</a> and <a href="/wiki/Ronald_Weasley" title="Ronald Weasley">Ron Weasley</a> as she helped him search. In Neville's third year, Professor Snape made him test his Shrinking Solution on the toad; though Neville's dubious potion-making skills could have resulted in the toad's death, Trevor was successfully transformed into a tadpole, much to the <a href="/wiki/Gryffindor" title="Gryffindor">Gryffindors</a>' delight.
</p><p>At some point, Trevor escaped into the Hogwarts Lake. Both pet and owner felt a sense of relief.<sup id="cite_ref-pottermore_61-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-pottermore-61">&#91;61&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Harry_Potter">Harry Potter</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Neville_Longbottom?veaction=edit&amp;section=24" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Harry Potter">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Neville_Longbottom?action=edit&amp;section=24" title="Edit section: Harry Potter"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Order of the Phoenix">"<i>Neville speaks most highly of you.</i>"</span></dd>
<dd>&#8212;Neville's high regard of Harry<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Order_of_the_Phoenix" title="Harry Potter and the Order of the Phoenix">[src]</a></sup></dd>
<dd></dd></dl></div>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 202px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/0/00/Harry_Potter_OOTPF.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20140702164312" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="200" height="288" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Harry Potter OOTPF.jpg" data-image-key="Harry_Potter_OOTPF.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/0/00/Harry_Potter_OOTPF.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/200?cb=20140702164312" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/0/00/Harry_Potter_OOTPF.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20140702164312" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/0/00/Harry_Potter_OOTPF.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/200?cb=20140702164312" decoding="async" width="200" height="288" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Harry Potter OOTPF.jpg" data-image-key="Harry_Potter_OOTPF.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/0/00/Harry_Potter_OOTPF.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/200?cb=20140702164312" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Harry_Potter_OOTPF.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter" title="Harry Potter">Harry Potter</a>, his good friend and room-mate</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Neville first met Harry Potter in <a href="/wiki/1991" title="1991">1991</a>, while Neville was looking for his toad, <a href="/wiki/Trevor" title="Trevor">Trevor</a>, on the <a href="/wiki/Hogwarts_Express" title="Hogwarts Express">Hogwarts Express</a>. They became classmates and room-mates after they were both sorted into the <a href="/wiki/Gryffindor" title="Gryffindor">Gryffindor</a> house, and came to be good friends over the years. In <a href="/wiki/1994" title="1994">1994</a>, Harry learned that Neville's parents were tortured into insanity by <a href="/wiki/Bartemius_Crouch_Junior" title="Bartemius Crouch Junior">Barty Crouch Jnr</a>, <a href="/wiki/Bellatrix_Lestrange" title="Bellatrix Lestrange">Bellatrix</a>, <a href="/wiki/Rodolphus_Lestrange" title="Rodolphus Lestrange">Rodolphus</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Rabastan_Lestrange" title="Rabastan Lestrange">Rabastan Lestrange</a>. Harry felt that Neville was far more deserving of pity than he, though he promised Dumbledore not to tell anyone what he knew, as it was Neville's decision whether or not to reveal his past to his friends.
</p><p>In their fifth year, Neville became a member of <a href="/wiki/Dumbledore%27s_Army" title="Dumbledore&#39;s Army">Dumbledore's Army</a>, an organisation led by Harry to oppose <a href="/wiki/Dolores_Umbridge" title="Dolores Umbridge">Dolores Umbridge</a> and learn practical <a href="/wiki/Defence_Against_the_Dark_Arts" title="Defence Against the Dark Arts">defensive magic</a>. After the <a href="/wiki/Lestranges" class="mw-redirect" title="Lestranges">Lestranges</a> escaped from <a href="/wiki/Azkaban" title="Azkaban">Azkaban</a> that same year, Neville resolved to become stronger and try to honour his parents' reputations as excellent Aurors. True to his word, Neville fought alongside Harry at the <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_the_Department_of_Mysteries" title="Battle of the Department of Mysteries">Battle of the Department of Mysteries</a> and saved Harry's life from <a href="/wiki/Walden_Macnair" title="Walden Macnair">Walden Macnair</a> when Macnair attempted to strangle Harry. When Harry was crying over the death of <a href="/wiki/Sirius_Black" title="Sirius Black">Sirius Black</a>, Neville did not question nor protest Harry's friendship with an alleged criminal and mass murder, instead consoling him for his godfather's demise.
</p><p>In <a href="/wiki/1996" title="1996">1996</a>, Harry refused to allow <a href="/wiki/Romilda_Vane" title="Romilda Vane">Romilda Vane</a> to insult Neville and <a href="/wiki/Luna_Lovegood" title="Luna Lovegood">Luna Lovegood</a>, stating that they were his real friends, and the only ones who had fought alongside Ron, Ginny, Hermione, and himself at the Department of Mysteries. At the end of the year, Neville and Harry both fought in the <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_the_Astronomy_Tower" title="Battle of the Astronomy Tower">Battle of the Astronomy Tower</a> and attended Dumbledore's <a href="/wiki/Funeral_of_Albus_Dumbledore" title="Funeral of Albus Dumbledore">funeral</a>.
</p>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows">"<i>The thing is, it helps when people stand up to them, it gives everyone hope. I used to notice that when you did it, Harry.</i>"</span></dd>
<dd>&#8212;Neville regarding how Harry inspires him<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Deathly_Hallows" title="Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows">[src]</a></sup></dd>
<dd></dd></dl></div>
<p>The next year, while Harry, Ron and Hermione left Hogwarts to search for Voldemort's <a href="/wiki/Horcrux" title="Horcrux">Horcruxes</a>, Neville, along with <a href="/wiki/Ginevra_Weasley" title="Ginevra Weasley">Ginny Weasley</a> and Luna Lovegood, led Dumbledore's Army in maintaining a steady level of opposition against <a href="/wiki/Alecto_and_Amycus_Carrow" title="Alecto and Amycus Carrow">Alecto and Amycus Carrow</a>, two Death Eaters who had been appointed deputy Headmaster and Headmistress of Hogwarts under <a href="/wiki/Severus_Snape" title="Severus Snape">Severus Snape</a>. Neville would later state that the hope Harry inspired in standing up to his enemies drove Neville to do the same. Neville and Harry fought together in the <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_Hogwarts" title="Battle of Hogwarts">Battle of Hogwarts</a>, where Harry realised that Neville was one of his closest friends and one of the few people he would like to see once again before he dies in the forest and Neville showed his bravery and loyalty to Harry when he openly defied Voldemort and beheaded <a href="/wiki/Nagini" title="Nagini">Nagini</a>, destroying Voldemort's last remaining Horcrux.
</p><p>Neville and Harry remained in contact after the end of the <a href="/wiki/Second_Wizarding_War" title="Second Wizarding War">Second Wizarding War</a> and Harry made Neville the godfather of his son <a href="/wiki/Albus_Potter" title="Albus Potter">Albus Severus</a>, showing their good friendship. Harry's children were later taught by Neville, who had been appointed <a href="/wiki/Herbology" title="Herbology">Herbology</a> professor at Hogwarts.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Hermione_Granger">Hermione Granger</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Neville_Longbottom?veaction=edit&amp;section=25" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Hermione Granger">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Neville_Longbottom?action=edit&amp;section=25" title="Edit section: Hermione Granger"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows"><b>Phineas Nigellus Black</b>: "<i>Exactly what claim did the Weasley girl have upon it? She deserved her punishment, as did the idiot Longbottom and the Lovegood oddity!</i>"</span></dd>
<dd><b>Hermione Granger</b>: "<i>Neville is not an idiot and Luna is not an oddity!</i>"</dd>
<dd>&#8212; Hermione Granger defending Neville and Luna to the <a href="/wiki/Portrait" title="Portrait">portrait</a> of <a href="/wiki/Phineas_Nigellus_Black" title="Phineas Nigellus Black">Phineas Nigellus Black</a><sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Deathly_Hallows" title="Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows">[src]</a></sup></dd></dl>
</div>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 182px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/2/21/Hermione_Granger_OOTP_profile.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20190117041925" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="180" height="253" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Hermione Granger OOTP profile.jpg" data-image-key="Hermione_Granger_OOTP_profile.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/2/21/Hermione_Granger_OOTP_profile.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20190117041925" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/2/21/Hermione_Granger_OOTP_profile.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20190117041925" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/2/21/Hermione_Granger_OOTP_profile.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20190117041925" decoding="async" width="180" height="253" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Hermione Granger OOTP profile.jpg" data-image-key="Hermione_Granger_OOTP_profile.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/2/21/Hermione_Granger_OOTP_profile.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20190117041925" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Hermione_Granger_OOTP_profile.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption"><a href="/wiki/Hermione_Granger" title="Hermione Granger">Hermione Granger</a>, his friend</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Neville met Hermione Granger on the <a href="/wiki/Hogwarts_Express" title="Hogwarts Express">Hogwarts Express</a> when she helped him find <a href="/wiki/Trevor" title="Trevor">Trevor</a>, his toad. During their years at <a href="/wiki/Hogwarts_School_of_Witchcraft_and_Wizardry" title="Hogwarts School of Witchcraft and Wizardry">Hogwarts</a>, they became closer as Hermione encouraged him to stand up for himself when <a href="/wiki/Draco_Malfoy" title="Draco Malfoy">Draco Malfoy</a> and his friends played pranks on him, or made jokes at his expense.
</p><p>Because of his lack of confidence in classes, Neville frequently made mistakes, and Hermione usually came to his assistance, often whispering instructions in his ear. She also took note of how shaken Neville was by their <a href="/wiki/Fourth_year" title="Fourth year">fourth year</a> lesson on the <a href="/wiki/Unforgivable_Curses" title="Unforgivable Curses">Unforgivable Curses</a>, shouting for <a href="/wiki/Bartemius_Crouch_Junior" title="Bartemius Crouch Junior">Professor Moody</a> to stop demonstrating the <a href="/wiki/Cruciatus_Curse" title="Cruciatus Curse">Cruciatus Curse</a> and later asking Neville if it was all right. Because Hermione had "<i>always been so nice</i>", Neville plucked up the courage to ask her to the <a href="/wiki/Yule_Ball" title="Yule Ball">Yule Ball</a> in <a href="/wiki/1994" title="1994">1994</a>, though she had already accepted the offer of <a href="/wiki/Viktor_Krum" title="Viktor Krum">Viktor Krum</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-GF23_33-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-GF23-33">&#91;33&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Neville and Hermione became members of <a href="/wiki/Dumbledore%27s_Army" title="Dumbledore&#39;s Army">Dumbledore's Army</a> in <a href="/wiki/1995" title="1995">1995</a>, during their fifth year at Hogwarts, and fought together at the <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_the_Department_of_Mysteries" title="Battle of the Department of Mysteries">Battle of the Department of Mysteries</a>, as well as in the <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_the_Astronomy_Tower" title="Battle of the Astronomy Tower">Battle of the Astronomy Tower</a> in <a href="/wiki/1997" title="1997">1997</a>. When the trio returned to Hogwarts in <a href="/wiki/1998" title="1998">1998</a> just before the <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_Hogwarts" title="Battle of Hogwarts">Battle of Hogwarts</a>, it was Neville who greeted them enthusiastically, and who first expressed a willingness to help them in any way possible and to fight the incoming <a href="/wiki/Death_Eaters" title="Death Eaters">Death Eater</a> army.
</p><p>After the <a href="/wiki/Second_Wizarding_War" title="Second Wizarding War">Second Wizarding War</a>, the two best friends remained in contact throughout the years.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Ron_Weasley">Ron Weasley</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Neville_Longbottom?veaction=edit&amp;section=26" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Ron Weasley">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Neville_Longbottom?action=edit&amp;section=26" title="Edit section: Ron Weasley"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows">"<i>Blimey, Neville, there’s a time and a place for getting a smart mouth!</i>"</span></dd>
<dd>&#8212;Ron to Neville after Neville explains how he received injuries at the hands of <a href="/wiki/Amycus_Carrow" title="Amycus Carrow">the</a> <a href="/wiki/Alecto_Carrow" title="Alecto Carrow">Carrows</a><sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Deathly_Hallows" title="Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows">[src]</a></sup></dd>
<dd></dd></dl></div>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 182px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/a/ab/0143ootp_ron.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20140702164633" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="180" height="272" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="0143ootp ron.jpg" data-image-key="0143ootp_ron.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/a/ab/0143ootp_ron.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20140702164633" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/a/ab/0143ootp_ron.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20140702164633" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/a/ab/0143ootp_ron.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20140702164633" decoding="async" width="180" height="272" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="0143ootp ron.jpg" data-image-key="0143ootp_ron.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/a/ab/0143ootp_ron.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20140702164633" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:0143ootp_ron.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption"><a href="/wiki/Ronald_Weasley" title="Ronald Weasley">Ron Weasley</a>, his friend and room-mate</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Neville met Ron Weasley on the <a href="/wiki/Hogwarts_Express" title="Hogwarts Express">Hogwarts Express</a> at the start of their <a href="/wiki/First_year" title="First year">first year</a>. As both were sorted into Gryffindor house, they became room-mates. Over time, Neville became good friends with Ron, who, like Hermione and Harry, encouraged Neville not to let the <a href="/wiki/Slytherin" title="Slytherin">Slytherins</a> get to him.
</p><p>Ron, Hermione, and <a href="/wiki/Ginevra_Weasley" title="Ginevra Weasley">Ginny</a> all learned about Neville's parents during their <a href="/wiki/Fifth_year" title="Fifth year">fifth year</a> at Hogwarts, and were shocked to learn that the good-natured, clumsy boy was carrying such a dark secret. Ron and Neville both became members of Dumbledore's Army in 1995, in order to oppose Professor Umbridge and learn to fight the <a href="/wiki/Death_Eaters" title="Death Eaters">Death Eaters</a>. They fought alongside one another at the <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_the_Department_of_Mysteries" title="Battle of the Department of Mysteries">Battle of the Department of Mysteries</a> and the <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_the_Astronomy_Tower" title="Battle of the Astronomy Tower">Battle of the Astronomy Tower</a>. Neville greeted Ron, Harry, and Hermione enthusiastically when they returned to Hogwarts in <a href="/wiki/1998" title="1998">1998</a>, and they all fought against Voldemort's forces in the <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_Hogwarts" title="Battle of Hogwarts">Battle of Hogwarts</a>. During the battle, Neville and Ron defeated <a href="/wiki/Fenrir_Greyback" title="Fenrir Greyback">Fenrir Greyback</a> together protecting each other, after the battle they remained as best friends and they regularly see each other.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Ginny_Weasley">Ginny Weasley</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Neville_Longbottom?veaction=edit&amp;section=27" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Ginny Weasley">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Neville_Longbottom?action=edit&amp;section=27" title="Edit section: Ginny Weasley"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 182px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/b/ba/1235081929_2852_full.jpeg/revision/latest?cb=20140627051728" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="180" height="256" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="1235081929 2852 full.jpeg" data-image-key="1235081929_2852_full.jpeg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/b/ba/1235081929_2852_full.jpeg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20140627051728" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/b/ba/1235081929_2852_full.jpeg/revision/latest?cb=20140627051728" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/b/ba/1235081929_2852_full.jpeg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20140627051728" decoding="async" width="180" height="256" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="1235081929 2852 full.jpeg" data-image-key="1235081929_2852_full.jpeg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/b/ba/1235081929_2852_full.jpeg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20140627051728" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:1235081929_2852_full.jpeg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption"><a href="/wiki/Ginevra_Weasley" title="Ginevra Weasley">Ginny Weasley</a>, a good friend and his <a href="/wiki/Yule_Ball" title="Yule Ball">Yule Ball</a> date</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>After asking Hermione to the Yule Ball in his fourth year and being turned down because she had already agreed to attend with <a href="/wiki/Viktor_Krum" title="Viktor Krum">Viktor Krum</a>, Neville asked Ginny Weasley. She agreed to go with him as a friend, being too young to attend otherwise.<sup id="cite_ref-GF23_33-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-GF23-33">&#91;33&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>The two continued to be friendly afterwards, and Ginny, like Harry, Hermione and Ron, encouraged Neville to be more confident. She and <a href="/wiki/Luna_Lovegood" title="Luna Lovegood">Luna Lovegood</a> were co-leaders of the re-formed <a href="/wiki/Dumbledore%27s_Army" title="Dumbledore&#39;s Army">Dumbledore's Army</a> along with Neville when Snape and the <a href="/wiki/Alecto_and_Amycus_Carrow" title="Alecto and Amycus Carrow">Carrows</a> controlled Hogwarts.<sup id="cite_ref-DH29_48-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-DH29-48">&#91;48&#93;</a></sup> Ginny and Neville also fought at the <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_the_Department_of_Mysteries" title="Battle of the Department of Mysteries">Battle of the Department of Mysteries</a>, the <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_the_Astronomy_Tower" title="Battle of the Astronomy Tower">Battle of the Astronomy Tower</a>, and the <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_Hogwarts" title="Battle of Hogwarts">Battle of Hogwarts</a> (where they blew up together the covered bridge).
</p><p>After the war, Ginny and Neville remained in contact, and they remained closest friends, with Ginny naming Neville godfather to her son <a href="/wiki/Albus_Potter" title="Albus Potter">Albus Severus</a> and being on friendly terms with her other son, <a href="/wiki/James_Potter_II" title="James Potter II">James Sirius</a>.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Luna_Lovegood">Luna Lovegood</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Neville_Longbottom?veaction=edit&amp;section=28" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Luna Lovegood">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Neville_Longbottom?action=edit&amp;section=28" title="Edit section: Luna Lovegood"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Order of the Phoenix"><b>Luna Lovegood</b>: "<i>And I don't know who you are.</i>"</span></dd>
<dd><b>Neville</b>: "<i>I'm nobody.</i>"</dd>
<dd><b>Ginny Weasley</b>: "<i>No, you're not. Neville Longbottom — Luna Lovegood...</i>"</dd>
<dd>&#8212; <a href="/wiki/Ginevra_Weasley" title="Ginevra Weasley">Ginny Weasley</a> introduces Neville and Luna<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Order_of_the_Phoenix" title="Harry Potter and the Order of the Phoenix">[src]</a></sup></dd></dl>
</div><figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 182px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/c/ca/Luna_HPHBP.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20100925141354" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="180" height="251" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Luna HPHBP.jpg" data-image-key="Luna_HPHBP.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/c/ca/Luna_HPHBP.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20100925141354" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/c/ca/Luna_HPHBP.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20100925141354" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/c/ca/Luna_HPHBP.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20100925141354" decoding="async" width="180" height="251" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Luna HPHBP.jpg" data-image-key="Luna_HPHBP.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/c/ca/Luna_HPHBP.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20100925141354" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Luna_HPHBP.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption"><a href="/wiki/Luna_Lovegood" title="Luna Lovegood">Luna Lovegood</a>, a good friend</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Neville and Luna, a <a href="/wiki/Ravenclaw" title="Ravenclaw">Ravenclaw</a> student, first met on the <a href="/wiki/Hogwarts_Express" title="Hogwarts Express">Hogwarts Express</a>, in <a href="/wiki/1995" title="1995">1995</a>. Neville found Luna a bit "<i>odd</i>", as she believed in the existence of strange, mythical creatures, had a tendency to read magazines upside down, and wore earrings that appeared to be made of radishes. Luna, like Harry and Neville, had the ability to see <a href="/wiki/Thestral" title="Thestral">Thestrals</a>, as they had all seen someone die.
</p><p>Spacey as Luna seemed, she fought alongside Neville at the <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_the_Department_of_Mysteries" title="Battle of the Department of Mysteries">Battle of the Department of Mysteries</a>, the <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_the_Astronomy_Tower" title="Battle of the Astronomy Tower">Battle of the Astronomy Tower</a>, and the <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_Hogwarts" title="Battle of Hogwarts">Battle of Hogwarts</a>. At some point they became very close friends. During Neville's last year at <a href="/wiki/Hogwarts_School_of_Witchcraft_and_Wizardry" title="Hogwarts School of Witchcraft and Wizardry">Hogwarts</a>, he, Luna and Ginny, re-formed and co-led <a href="/wiki/Dumbledore%27s_Army" title="Dumbledore&#39;s Army">Dumbledore's Army</a> in order to oppose the <a href="/wiki/Alecto_and_Amycus_Carrow" title="Alecto and Amycus Carrow">Carrows</a>. Neville seems to have a place in his heart for Luna, they also remained close friends in later life. It seemed that Luna was always glad when Neville, Ginny, Hermione, Ron, and Harry were close by, proved when the trio visited Luna's father <a href="/wiki/Xenophilius_Lovegood" title="Xenophilius Lovegood">Xenophilius Lovegood</a> and seeing Luna's room with their painting on her bedroom ceiling connected with gold letters spelling "<i>friends</i>".
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Draco_Malfoy">Draco Malfoy</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Neville_Longbottom?veaction=edit&amp;section=29" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Draco Malfoy">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Neville_Longbottom?action=edit&amp;section=29" title="Edit section: Draco Malfoy"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 182px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/1/1b/Draco_Malfoy_Promo_HPB.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20140623200502" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="180" height="266" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Draco Malfoy Promo HPB.jpg" data-image-key="Draco_Malfoy_Promo_HPB.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/1/1b/Draco_Malfoy_Promo_HPB.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20140623200502" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/1/1b/Draco_Malfoy_Promo_HPB.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20140623200502" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/1/1b/Draco_Malfoy_Promo_HPB.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20140623200502" decoding="async" width="180" height="266" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Draco Malfoy Promo HPB.jpg" data-image-key="Draco_Malfoy_Promo_HPB.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/1/1b/Draco_Malfoy_Promo_HPB.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20140623200502" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Draco_Malfoy_Promo_HPB.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption"><a href="/wiki/Draco_Malfoy" title="Draco Malfoy">Draco Malfoy</a>, his school bully</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Philosopher&#39;s Stone">"<i>Longbottom, if brains were gold you'd be poorer than <a href="/wiki/Ronald_Weasley" title="Ronald Weasley">Weasley</a>, and that's saying something.</i>"</span></dd>
<dd>&#8212;Draco Malfoy's opinion of Neville<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Philosopher%27s_Stone" title="Harry Potter and the Philosopher&#39;s Stone">[src]</a></sup></dd>
<dd></dd></dl></div>
<p>Initially shy and clumsy, Neville regularly found himself on the receiving end of insults from Draco and his <a href="/wiki/Draco_Malfoy%27s_gang" title="Draco Malfoy&#39;s gang">gang</a>, and was often the butt of their jokes and pranks — a fact which served only to make Neville clumsier and less confident. When encouraged by Hermione, Ron, and Harry to stand up for himself, Neville replied with "<i>how I can barely stand at all</i>" but, despite this previous mind set Neville grew to be someone who was much more difficult to bully by his later years at Hogwarts.
</p><p>He started resisting against not only the Slytherin students, but also <a href="/wiki/Alecto_and_Amycus_Carrow" title="Alecto and Amycus Carrow">Alecto and Amycus Carrow</a> and <a href="/wiki/Severus_Snape" title="Severus Snape">Severus Snape</a>. During the <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_Hogwarts" title="Battle of Hogwarts">Battle of Hogwarts</a>, Neville proved to have made an impressive and complete turn around from his earlier years of crumbling under Draco's bullying, when he openly defied <a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle" title="Tom Riddle">Lord Voldemort</a> and beheaded <a href="/wiki/Nagini" title="Nagini">Nagini</a>, effectively destroying Voldemort's final <a href="/wiki/Horcrux" title="Horcrux">Horcrux</a>.
</p>
<h3><span id="Dumbledore's_Army"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Dumbledore.27s_Army">Dumbledore's Army</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Neville_Longbottom?veaction=edit&amp;section=30" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Dumbledore&#039;s Army">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Neville_Longbottom?action=edit&amp;section=30" title="Edit section: Dumbledore&#039;s Army"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Half-blood Prince">"<i>I liked the D.A.! I learned </i>loads<i> with you!</i>"</span></dd>
<dd>&#8212;Neville to <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter" title="Harry Potter">Harry Potter</a> on D.A. meetings<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Half-blood_Prince" class="mw-redirect" title="Harry Potter and the Half-blood Prince">[src]</a></sup></dd>
<dd></dd></dl></div>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 252px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/9/96/Dumbledore%27s_Army.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20161123060553" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="250" height="166" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Dumbledore&#39;s Army.jpg" data-image-key="Dumbledore&#39;s_Army.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/9/96/Dumbledore%27s_Army.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20161123060553" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/9/96/Dumbledore%27s_Army.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20161123060553" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/9/96/Dumbledore%27s_Army.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20161123060553" decoding="async" width="250" height="166" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Dumbledore&#39;s Army.jpg" data-image-key="Dumbledore&#39;s_Army.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/9/96/Dumbledore%27s_Army.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20161123060553" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Dumbledore%27s_Army.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption"><a href="/wiki/Dumbledore%27s_Army" title="Dumbledore&#39;s Army">Dumbledore's Army</a>, his friends and allies</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Dumbledore's Army was an organisation led by Harry Potter that sought not only to undermine the dictatorial authority of <a href="/wiki/Dolores_Umbridge" title="Dolores Umbridge">Dolores Umbridge</a>, but to offer students a means of learning the practical defensive magic Umbridge denied them in their actual <a href="/wiki/Defence_Against_the_Dark_Arts" title="Defence Against the Dark Arts">Defence Against the Dark Arts</a> class. Neville became a member at the time of its formation in 1995, and this marked something of a turning point both in terms Neville's relationships with other Hogwarts students, and in terms of his magical ability beyond <a href="/wiki/Herbology" title="Herbology">Herbology</a>. As the D.A.'s practice progressed throughout the course of the year, Neville showed marked improvement in his ability to <a href="/wiki/Disarming_Charm" title="Disarming Charm">disarm</a> and <a href="/wiki/Stunning_Spell" title="Stunning Spell">stun</a>, as well as perform the <a href="/wiki/Impediment_Jinx" title="Impediment Jinx">Impediment Jinx</a> and <a href="/wiki/Reductor_Curse" title="Reductor Curse">Reductor Curse</a>, among others.
</p><p>When several <a href="/wiki/Death_Eaters" title="Death Eaters">Death Eaters</a> <a href="/wiki/Azkaban_escapes" title="Azkaban escapes">escaped</a> from <a href="/wiki/Azkaban" title="Azkaban">Azkaban</a> in early 1996, all of the D.A. pushed themselves to improve their duelling abilities, but none more than Neville, as three of the escapees had taken part in torturing his parents into insanity.
</p><p>While training with the D.A.equipped Neville to face the <a href="/wiki/Death_Eaters" title="Death Eaters">Death Eaters</a> in the <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_the_Department_of_Mysteries" title="Battle of the Department of Mysteries">Battle of the Department of Mysteries</a>, the sense of camaraderie Neville enjoyed with them made him one of only three members (along with <a href="/wiki/Ginevra_Weasley" title="Ginevra Weasley">Ginny Weasley</a> and <a href="/wiki/Luna_Lovegood" title="Luna Lovegood">Luna Lovegood</a>) to answer Ron and Hermione's call leading up to the <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_the_Astronomy_Tower" title="Battle of the Astronomy Tower">Battle of the Astronomy Tower</a>.
</p><p>Neville, Ginny and Luna co-led the DA in 1997, when it was re-formed to oppose the reign of Severus Snape, Alecto Carrow, and Amycus Carrow at Hogwarts. Most of the former members reunited and spent ample time hiding in the <a href="/wiki/Room_of_Requirement" title="Room of Requirement">Room of Requirement</a>, awaiting the return of Harry, Ron, and Hermione. They were quick to mobilise against the invading Death Eaters, with Neville at their lead, while Harry, Ron, and Hermione were searching for <a href="/wiki/Rowena_Ravenclaw%27s_Diadem" class="mw-redirect" title="Rowena Ravenclaw&#39;s Diadem">Rowena Ravenclaw's Diadem</a>. While Fred Weasley, Lavender Brown and Colin Creevey were tragically killed, Neville fought valiantly and eventually beheaded <a href="/wiki/Nagini" title="Nagini">Nagini</a> on Harry's orders, destroyed Voldemort's final remaining <a href="/wiki/Horcrux" title="Horcrux">Horcrux</a>.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Bellatrix_Lestrange">Bellatrix Lestrange</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Neville_Longbottom?veaction=edit&amp;section=31" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Bellatrix Lestrange">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Neville_Longbottom?action=edit&amp;section=31" title="Edit section: Bellatrix Lestrange"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Order of the Phoenix"><b>Bellatrix</b>: "<i>Longbottom? Why, I have had the pleasure of meeting your parents, boy. . . .</i>"</span></dd>
<dd><b>Neville</b>: "<i>I DOE YOU HAB!</i>"</dd>
<dd>&#8212; Bellatrix taunting Neville during the Battle of the Department of Mysteries<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Order_of_the_Phoenix" title="Harry Potter and the Order of the Phoenix">[src]</a></sup></dd></dl>
</div>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 182px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/3/31/Bellatrix-promo-bellatrix-lestrange-28967562-470-627.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20140619032053" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="180" height="240" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Bellatrix-promo-bellatrix-lestrange-28967562-470-627.jpg" data-image-key="Bellatrix-promo-bellatrix-lestrange-28967562-470-627.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/3/31/Bellatrix-promo-bellatrix-lestrange-28967562-470-627.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20140619032053" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/3/31/Bellatrix-promo-bellatrix-lestrange-28967562-470-627.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20140619032053" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/3/31/Bellatrix-promo-bellatrix-lestrange-28967562-470-627.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20140619032053" decoding="async" width="180" height="240" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Bellatrix-promo-bellatrix-lestrange-28967562-470-627.jpg" data-image-key="Bellatrix-promo-bellatrix-lestrange-28967562-470-627.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/3/31/Bellatrix-promo-bellatrix-lestrange-28967562-470-627.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20140619032053" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Bellatrix-promo-bellatrix-lestrange-28967562-470-627.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption"><a href="/wiki/Bellatrix_Lestrange" title="Bellatrix Lestrange">Bellatrix Lestrange</a>, a hated enemy and the witch who helped torture his parents into insanity</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Bellatrix Lestrange led fellow <a href="/wiki/Death_Eaters" title="Death Eaters">Death Eaters</a>; <a href="/wiki/Rodolphus_Lestrange" title="Rodolphus Lestrange">Rodolphus Lestrange</a>, <a href="/wiki/Rabastan_Lestrange" title="Rabastan Lestrange">Rabastan Lestrange</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Bartemius_Crouch_Junior" title="Bartemius Crouch Junior">Barty Crouch Jnr</a> in the torture Neville's parents by means of the <a href="/wiki/Cruciatus_Curse" title="Cruciatus Curse">Cruciatus Curse</a>, leaving them permanently incapacitated in <a href="/wiki/St_Mungo%27s_Hospital_for_Magical_Maladies_and_Injuries" title="St Mungo&#39;s Hospital for Magical Maladies and Injuries">St Mungo's</a>. When Bellatrix <a href="/wiki/Azkaban_escapes" title="Azkaban escapes">escaped</a> from <a href="/wiki/Azkaban" title="Azkaban">Azkaban</a> prison in January <a href="/wiki/1996" title="1996">1996</a>, Neville was heavily affected.
</p><p>His performance in <a href="/wiki/Dumbledore%27s_Army" title="Dumbledore&#39;s Army">Dumbledore's Army</a> increased to the point where he managed to master the <a href="/wiki/Shield_Charm" title="Shield Charm">Shield Charm</a> before everyone but <a href="/wiki/Hermione_Granger" title="Hermione Granger">Hermione</a>. When he <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_the_Department_of_Mysteries" title="Battle of the Department of Mysteries">went to the Ministry of Magic</a> later that year, Bellatrix taunted him about his parents, but Neville fought back, much to Bellatrix's surprise. Neville also saw Bellatrix murder <a href="/wiki/Sirius_Black" title="Sirius Black">Sirius Black</a>, and expressed his condolences to Harry. Neville met Bellatrix again in <a href="/wiki/1998" title="1998">1998</a>, during the <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_Hogwarts" title="Battle of Hogwarts">Battle of Hogwarts</a>, where she was eventually killed in a duel by <a href="/wiki/Molly_Weasley" title="Molly Weasley">Molly Weasley</a>.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Severus_Snape">Severus Snape</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Neville_Longbottom?veaction=edit&amp;section=32" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Severus Snape">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Neville_Longbottom?action=edit&amp;section=32" title="Edit section: Severus Snape"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Prisoner of Azkaban">"<i>Tell me, boy, does anything penetrate that thick skull of yours? Didn’t you hear me say, quite clearly, that only one rat spleen was needed? Didn’t I state plainly that a dash of leech juice would suffice? What do I have to do to make you understand, Longbottom?”</i>"</span></dd>
<dd>&#8212;Snape tormenting Neville<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Prisoner_of_Azkaban" title="Harry Potter and the Prisoner of Azkaban">[src]</a></sup></dd>
<dd></dd></dl></div>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 182px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/8/8b/Severus_Snape_Profile.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20081103135333" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="180" height="254" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Severus Snape Profile.jpg" data-image-key="Severus_Snape_Profile.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/8/8b/Severus_Snape_Profile.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20081103135333" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/8/8b/Severus_Snape_Profile.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20081103135333" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/8/8b/Severus_Snape_Profile.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20081103135333" decoding="async" width="180" height="254" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Severus Snape Profile.jpg" data-image-key="Severus_Snape_Profile.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/8/8b/Severus_Snape_Profile.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20081103135333" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Severus_Snape_Profile.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption"><a href="/wiki/Severus_Snape" title="Severus Snape">Severus Snape</a>, his professor and <a href="/wiki/Boggart" title="Boggart">Boggart</a></p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>During his years at school, Neville was terrified of Professor Severus Snape, and the poor boy managed to earn the <a href="/wiki/Potions_Master" title="Potions Master">Potions Master</a>'s ire in almost every lesson. Snape regularly and unnecessarily targeted Neville with verbal taunts, threats, sarcasm, and malice, which put an extremely nervous Neville even more on edge. Snape went so far as to feed a few drops of Neville's <a href="/wiki/Shrinking_Solution" title="Shrinking Solution">Shrinking Solution</a> to Neville's pet, <a href="/wiki/Trevor" title="Trevor">Trevor</a>, so as to humiliate him for doing badly on the potion and almost kill Neville's toad. Thanks to Hermione, Neville was able to fix his potion so that his toad wasn't harmed.
</p><p>Neville admitted in <a href="/wiki/1993" title="1993">1993</a> that Snape scared him more than anything else in the world, and was the form his <a href="/wiki/Boggart" title="Boggart">boggart</a> took. When <a href="/wiki/Remus_Lupin" title="Remus Lupin">Professor Lupin</a> asked the <a href="/wiki/Defence_Against_the_Dark_Arts" title="Defence Against the Dark Arts">Defence Against the Dark Arts</a> class what frightened them the most, Neville at first mumbled inaudibly; when Professor Lupin asked Neville to say it clearly, Neville (after wildly looking around) whispered "<i>Professor Snape</i>." Nearly everyone laughed at that, and then Professor Lupin replied thoughtfully, "<i>Professor Snape</i>."<sup id="cite_ref-PA7_7-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-PA7-7">&#91;7&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>When he sat his <a href="/wiki/Potions_(class)" title="Potions (class)">Potions</a> <a href="/wiki/Ordinary_Wizarding_Level" title="Ordinary Wizarding Level">O.W.L.</a> in <a href="/wiki/1996" title="1996">1996</a>, Harry noted that Neville looked happier than usual without Snape around. Neville also co-led the second <a href="/wiki/Dumbledore%27s_Army" title="Dumbledore&#39;s Army">Dumbledore's Army</a> and wrote slogans on the walls, in order to oppose Snape and the Carrows. Snape was killed by Nagini during the <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_Hogwarts" title="Battle of Hogwarts">Battle of Hogwarts</a>. Though Neville was present when Harry informed Voldemort of Snape's true allegiance, it is unknown how Neville reacted. It is possible Snape hated Neville so much because if Voldemort had chosen to go after him rather than Harry, Lily would still be alive.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Albus_Dumbledore">Albus Dumbledore</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Neville_Longbottom?veaction=edit&amp;section=33" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Albus Dumbledore">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Neville_Longbottom?action=edit&amp;section=33" title="Edit section: Albus Dumbledore"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Philosopher&#39;s Stone">"<i>There are all kinds of courage. It takes a great deal of bravery to stand up to our enemies, but just as much to stand up to our friends. I therefore award ten points to Mr Neville Longbottom.</i>"</span></dd>
<dd>&#8212;Albus Dumbledore rewarding Neville's bravery<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Philosopher%27s_Stone" title="Harry Potter and the Philosopher&#39;s Stone">[src]</a></sup></dd>
<dd></dd></dl></div>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 182px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/0/09/600full-Albus-Dumbledore-the-prisoner-of-azkaban-photo.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20141122220412" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="180" height="244" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="600full-Albus-Dumbledore-the-prisoner-of-azkaban-photo.jpg" data-image-key="600full-Albus-Dumbledore-the-prisoner-of-azkaban-photo.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/0/09/600full-Albus-Dumbledore-the-prisoner-of-azkaban-photo.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20141122220412" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/0/09/600full-Albus-Dumbledore-the-prisoner-of-azkaban-photo.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20141122220412" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/0/09/600full-Albus-Dumbledore-the-prisoner-of-azkaban-photo.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20141122220412" decoding="async" width="180" height="244" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="600full-Albus-Dumbledore-the-prisoner-of-azkaban-photo.jpg" data-image-key="600full-Albus-Dumbledore-the-prisoner-of-azkaban-photo.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/0/09/600full-Albus-Dumbledore-the-prisoner-of-azkaban-photo.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20141122220412" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:600full-Albus-Dumbledore-the-prisoner-of-azkaban-photo.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption"><a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore" title="Albus Dumbledore">Albus Dumbledore</a>, his headmaster</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Neville thought Albus Dumbledore was the greatest <a href="/wiki/Wizardkind" title="Wizardkind">wizard</a> of all time. He met Dumbledore in <a href="/wiki/1991" title="1991">1991</a>, when he was the headmaster of <a href="/wiki/Hogwarts_School_of_Witchcraft_and_Wizardry" title="Hogwarts School of Witchcraft and Wizardry">Hogwarts</a>. At the end of Neville's first year, Dumbledore awarded <a href="/wiki/Gryffindor" title="Gryffindor">Gryffindor</a> the ten points they needed to win the House cup because Neville had the courage to try and stop <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter" title="Harry Potter">Harry</a>, <a href="/wiki/Hermione_Granger" title="Hermione Granger">Hermione</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Ronald_Weasley" title="Ronald Weasley">Ron</a> from leaving the Gryffindor tower after hours. Dumbledore also knew about Neville's parents, and told Harry not to say anything, leaving Neville the right to choose when he revealed his past to his friends.
</p><p>Dumbledore and Neville also fought together at the <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_the_Department_of_Mysteries" title="Battle of the Department of Mysteries">Battle of the Department of Mysteries</a>, and the <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_the_Astronomy_Tower" title="Battle of the Astronomy Tower">Battle of the Astronomy Tower</a>, where Dumbledore was killed by Severus Snape. Neville was devastated by his death. Neville despised professor <a href="/wiki/Dolores_Umbridge" title="Dolores Umbridge">Dolores Umbridge</a>, the <a href="/wiki/British_Ministry_of_Magic" title="British Ministry of Magic">Ministry</a>-appointed <a href="/wiki/Defence_Against_the_Dark_Arts" title="Defence Against the Dark Arts">Defence Against the Dark Arts</a> professor for the <a href="/wiki/1995%E2%80%931996_school_year" title="1995–1996 school year">1995–1996 school year</a>. Like nearly everyone else at Hogwarts, with the possible exception of some of the <a href="/wiki/Slytherin" title="Slytherin">Slytherin</a> students and <a href="/wiki/Argus_Filch" title="Argus Filch">Argus Filch</a>, Neville hated Umbridge for her sadistic punishments and attempts to control the school. He became a member of <a href="/wiki/Dumbledore%27s_Army" title="Dumbledore&#39;s Army">Dumbledore's Army</a> partially in order to oppose her. Umbridge left the school in 1996 after paying the price for verbally assaulting a herd of centaurs and attempting to flee; she was discovered by Peeves, who led the students in chasing her away from the school.
</p><p><a href="/wiki/Death_Eaters" title="Death Eaters">Death Eaters</a> <a href="/wiki/Alecto_and_Amycus_Carrow" title="Alecto and Amycus Carrow">Alecto and Amycus Carrow</a> were appointed professors at Hogwarts in <a href="/wiki/1997" title="1997">1997</a>, after Dumbledore's <a href="/wiki/Death" title="Death">death</a>. Amycus taught Defence Against the Dark Arts, which he changed to the <a href="/wiki/Dark_Arts" title="Dark Arts">Dark Arts</a>, and Alecto taught <a href="/wiki/Muggle_Studies" title="Muggle Studies">Muggle Studies</a> with an obvious anti-Muggle slant. Amycus and Alecto liked to punish the students with the use of torture, and ordered students to practise the <a href="/wiki/Cruciatus_Curse" title="Cruciatus Curse">Cruciatus Curse</a> on other students who had been detained. Neville helped re-form Dumbledore's Army, along with Ginny and Luna, and maintained a steady opposition against the Carrows throughout the course of the year. In an attempt to control Neville, Ministry Auror John Dawlish was sent to take Neville's grandmother hostage; unfortunately for Dawlish, the tenacious Augusta Longbottom fought back, apparently putting Dawlish in St Mungo's and going on the run. As the Carrows no longer had hope of finding any real leverage to use against Neville, and had no reason not to simply kill him, Neville went into hiding in the Room of Requirement, where he was soon joined by a number of other Gryffindor, <a href="/wiki/Hufflepuff" title="Hufflepuff">Hufflepuff</a> and <a href="/wiki/Ravenclaw" title="Ravenclaw">Ravenclaw</a> students who saw fit to do the same.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Hogwarts_staff">Hogwarts staff</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Neville_Longbottom?veaction=edit&amp;section=34" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Hogwarts staff">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Neville_Longbottom?action=edit&amp;section=34" title="Edit section: Hogwarts staff"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Half-Blood Prince">"<i>It’s high time your grandmother learned to be proud of the grandson she’s got, rather than the one she thinks she ought to have - particularly after what happened at the Ministry.</i>"</span></dd>
<dd>&#8212;Minerva praising Neville's abilities<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Half-Blood_Prince" title="Harry Potter and the Half-Blood Prince">[src]</a></sup></dd>
<dd></dd></dl></div>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 182px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/f/fe/Minerva_McGonagall_POAF_promo.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20140521115100" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="180" height="253" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Minerva McGonagall POAF promo.jpg" data-image-key="Minerva_McGonagall_POAF_promo.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/f/fe/Minerva_McGonagall_POAF_promo.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20140521115100" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/f/fe/Minerva_McGonagall_POAF_promo.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20140521115100" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/f/fe/Minerva_McGonagall_POAF_promo.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20140521115100" decoding="async" width="180" height="253" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Minerva McGonagall POAF promo.jpg" data-image-key="Minerva_McGonagall_POAF_promo.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/f/fe/Minerva_McGonagall_POAF_promo.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20140521115100" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Minerva_McGonagall_POAF_promo.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption"><a href="/wiki/Minerva_McGonagall" title="Minerva McGonagall">Professor McGonagall</a>, his Head of House and professor</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Minerva McGonagall was Neville's Head of <a href="/wiki/Gryffindor" title="Gryffindor">House</a> and Transfiguration professor during his years at <a href="/wiki/Hogwarts_School_of_Witchcraft_and_Wizardry" title="Hogwarts School of Witchcraft and Wizardry">Hogwarts</a>. She often scolded Neville for his clumsiness and incompetence, though it was more likely his lack of confidence that frustrated her. McGonagall knew that Neville was capable of more than he seemed and saw that he was actually brave, and thus encouraged him to work to his potential. She was also a friend of Neville's <a href="/wiki/Augusta_Longbottom" title="Augusta Longbottom">grandmother</a>, and had known his parents in their days as Aurors. Neville and McGonagall both fought in the <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_the_Astronomy_Tower" title="Battle of the Astronomy Tower">Battle of the Astronomy Tower</a> and the <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_Hogwarts" title="Battle of Hogwarts">Battle of Hogwarts</a>, and both survived the war. Years after the war, Neville was given the position of Herbology professor at Hogwarts, although it is unknown if McGonagall was still teaching there.
</p>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 182px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/7/71/PSprout.png/revision/latest?cb=20110109155242" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="180" height="283" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="PSprout.png" data-image-key="PSprout.png" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/7/71/PSprout.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20110109155242" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/7/71/PSprout.png/revision/latest?cb=20110109155242" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/7/71/PSprout.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20110109155242" decoding="async" width="180" height="283" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="PSprout.png" data-image-key="PSprout.png" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/7/71/PSprout.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20110109155242" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:PSprout.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption"><a href="/wiki/Pomona_Sprout" title="Pomona Sprout">Professor Sprout</a>, his Herbology professor</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Professor Sprout was Neville's <a href="/wiki/Herbology" title="Herbology">Herbology</a> professor, and as Neville proved to be quite adept at Herbology, possibly the best in the year, she was undoubtedly the Professor he got along with best. At one point, Sprout even spoke of Neville's strength in the subject to <a href="/wiki/Bartemius_Crouch_Junior" title="Bartemius Crouch Junior">Barty Crouch Jnr</a>, while he was disguised as <a href="/wiki/Alastor_Moody" title="Alastor Moody">Professor Moody</a>. Neville helped Sprout use <a href="/wiki/Devil%27s_Snare" title="Devil&#39;s Snare">Devil's Snare</a>, <a href="/wiki/Mandrake" title="Mandrake">Mandrakes</a>, <a href="/wiki/Venomous_Tentacula" title="Venomous Tentacula">Venomous Tentacula</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Snargaluff" title="Snargaluff">Snargaluff</a> pods to attack the <a href="/wiki/Death_Eaters" title="Death Eaters">Death Eaters</a> during the Battle of Hogwarts, and they both survived the war. It is likely that Sprout had retired by the time Neville was appointed the new Herbology Professor, though they may have taught the class together.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Bartemius_Crouch_Jnr">Bartemius Crouch Jnr</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Neville_Longbottom?veaction=edit&amp;section=35" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Bartemius Crouch Jnr">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Neville_Longbottom?action=edit&amp;section=35" title="Edit section: Bartemius Crouch Jnr"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Goblet of Fire">"<i>It’s all right, sonny. Why don’t you come up to my office? Come on... we can have a cup of <a href="/wiki/Tea" title="Tea">tea</a>....</i>"</span></dd>
<dd>&#8212;Barty Crouch (as <a href="/wiki/Alastor_Moody" title="Alastor Moody">Alastor Moody</a>) pretending to comfort Neville after showing him the <a href="/wiki/Cruciatus_Curse" title="Cruciatus Curse">Cruciatus Curse</a><sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Goblet_of_Fire" title="Harry Potter and the Goblet of Fire">[src]</a></sup></dd>
<dd></dd></dl></div>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 182px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/b/b8/Barty_Crouch_Jnr_cropped.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20100301190039" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="180" height="260" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Barty Crouch Jnr cropped.jpg" data-image-key="Barty_Crouch_Jnr_cropped.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/b/b8/Barty_Crouch_Jnr_cropped.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20100301190039" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/b/b8/Barty_Crouch_Jnr_cropped.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20100301190039" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/b/b8/Barty_Crouch_Jnr_cropped.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20100301190039" decoding="async" width="180" height="260" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Barty Crouch Jnr cropped.jpg" data-image-key="Barty_Crouch_Jnr_cropped.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/b/b8/Barty_Crouch_Jnr_cropped.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20100301190039" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Barty_Crouch_Jnr_cropped.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption"><a href="/wiki/Bartemius_Crouch_Junior" title="Bartemius Crouch Junior">Bartemius Crouch Jnr</a>, who helped torture his parents into insanity</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Barty Crouch Jnr was also involved in the torture of Neville's parents by means of the <a href="/wiki/Cruciatus_Curse" title="Cruciatus Curse">Cruciatus Curse</a>. During Neville's <a href="/wiki/Fourth_year" title="Fourth year">fourth year</a>, Barty impersonated <a href="/wiki/Alastor_Moody" title="Alastor Moody">Alastor Moody</a> and served as Neville's <a href="/wiki/Defence_Against_the_Dark_Arts" title="Defence Against the Dark Arts">Defence Against the Dark Arts</a> Professor.
</p><p>During his first lesson with the fourth years, Barty (as Moody) took notice of Neville's name on the class register. He then demonstrated the three <a href="/wiki/Unforgivable_Curses" title="Unforgivable Curses">Unforgivable Curses</a> on spiders, including the Cruciatus Curse, which left Neville deeply shaken. "Moody" afterwards had tea with Neville and gave him a <a href="/wiki/Goshawk%27s_Guide_to_Herbology" title="Goshawk&#39;s Guide to Herbology">book</a> about <a href="/wiki/Herbology" title="Herbology">Herbology</a>, seemingly out of comfort and support, although it was later revealed that he had only done so to give Harry a clue about the <a href="/wiki/Triwizard_Tournament" title="Triwizard Tournament">Triwizard Tournament</a>'s second task. It is unknown how Neville reacted upon learning the truth about his D.A.D.A. teacher. Barty Crouch was given the <a href="/wiki/Dementor%27s_Kiss" title="Dementor&#39;s Kiss">Dementor's Kiss</a> in <a href="/wiki/1995" title="1995">1995</a>, losing his <a href="/wiki/Soul" title="Soul">soul</a>.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Lord_Voldemort">Lord Voldemort</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Neville_Longbottom?veaction=edit&amp;section=36" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Lord Voldemort">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Neville_Longbottom?action=edit&amp;section=36" title="Edit section: Lord Voldemort"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows"><b>Lord Voldemort</b>: "<i>You show spirit and bravery, and you come of noble stock. You will make a very valuable Death Eater. We need your kind, Neville Longbottom.</i>"</span></dd>
<dd><b>Neville</b>: "<i>I'll join you when hell freezes over! Dumbledore's Army!</i>"</dd>
<dd>&#8212; Voldemort and Neville at the Battle of Hogwarts<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Deathly_Hallows" title="Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows">[src]</a></sup></dd></dl>
</div>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 182px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/5/59/Tom_Riddle_DHF2.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20140630194830" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="180" height="251" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Tom Riddle DHF2.jpg" data-image-key="Tom_Riddle_DHF2.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/5/59/Tom_Riddle_DHF2.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20140630194830" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/5/59/Tom_Riddle_DHF2.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20140630194830" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/5/59/Tom_Riddle_DHF2.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20140630194830" decoding="async" width="180" height="251" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Tom Riddle DHF2.jpg" data-image-key="Tom_Riddle_DHF2.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/5/59/Tom_Riddle_DHF2.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20140630194830" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Tom_Riddle_DHF2.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption"><a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle" title="Tom Riddle">Lord Voldemort</a>, an enemy</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Neville was one of the two boys possibly referred to in <a href="/wiki/Sybill_Trelawney%27s_first_prophecy" title="Sybill Trelawney&#39;s first prophecy">the prophecy</a> as being destined to bring about Voldemort's end. However, Voldemort chose to target the <a href="/wiki/Potter_family" title="Potter family">Potters</a> based on the simple concept that Harry was a half-blood like himself, thus marking Harry, and not Neville, as his equal. After Lord Voldemort's first defeat, four fanatically loyal <a href="/wiki/Death_Eaters" title="Death Eaters">Death Eaters</a> tortured Neville's parents, <a href="/wiki/Frank_Longbottom" title="Frank Longbottom">Frank</a> and <a href="/wiki/Alice_Longbottom" title="Alice Longbottom">Alice Longbottom</a>, to the point of insanity, using the <a href="/wiki/Cruciatus_Curse" title="Cruciatus Curse">Cruciatus Curse</a>, in an attempt to force Voldemort's whereabouts out of them; this fact initially haunted Neville, but eventually spurred him to rise to his full potential.
</p><p>After honing his skills and steadily acquiring self-confidence through training with <a href="/wiki/Dumbledore%27s_Army" title="Dumbledore&#39;s Army">Dumbledore's Army</a>, Neville fought against Voldemort's Death Eaters countless times during the <a href="/wiki/Second_Wizarding_War" title="Second Wizarding War">Second Wizarding War</a>. Near the end of the <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_Hogwarts" title="Battle of Hogwarts">Battle of Hogwarts</a>, Neville actually attempted to charge directly at Voldemort, presumably aiming to slay <a href="/wiki/Nagini" title="Nagini">Nagini</a>, as Harry had told him she had to die at all costs. Voldemort offered Neville the chance to join him, commending his "<i>spirit and bravery</i>;" Neville declined, and instead, drew the <a href="/wiki/Sword_of_Gryffindor" title="Sword of Gryffindor">Sword of Gryffindor</a> from the <a href="/wiki/Sorting_Hat" title="Sorting Hat">Sorting Hat</a> and succeeded in beheading Nagini. As Nagini had been Voldemort's last remaining Horcrux, Neville's incredible display of bravery allowed Harry to defeat Voldemort once and for all.
</p><p>In addition to this, Neville also indirectly fulfilled his role in the prophecy by destroying Voldemort's last remaining Horcrux as it was this act which allowed Harry to finally defeat Voldemort. Although Voldemort chose to mark Harry as his target based on the prophecy, Neville proved by standing up to him and destroying his final Horcrux that he was almost exactly capable of being the other boy to meet the prophecy's requirements. It is unknown whether Voldemort recognised Neville as the other boy which the prophecy referred to and it is also unknown if Neville ever learnt this himself after Voldemort's final defeat.
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Neville_Longbottom?veaction=edit&amp;section=37" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Etymology">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Neville_Longbottom?action=edit&amp;section=37" title="Edit section: Etymology"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<ul><li>Neville is an English name originally derived from Norman French for "new town".<sup id="cite_ref-62" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-62">&#91;62&#93;</a></sup> It was the surname of a noble and a powerful warrior lineage family prominent in England in the medieval period, as well as the given name of a Prime Minister of Britain, <a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Neville_Chamberlain" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Neville Chamberlain">Neville Chamberlain</a>, whose role in history is controversial. Neville Chamberlain is infamous for his policy of appeasing dictator Adolf Hitler just prior to World War II, which is ironic, considering that Neville Longbottom never faltered in his defiance of Lord Voldemort.</li>
<li>Longbottom is the name of one of the Hobbits' villages at the <a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Shire" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Shire">Shire</a>, known for its best pipe-weed.</li>
<li>Longbottom is a family name around Bristol, where JK Rowling spent part of her childhood.</li></ul>
