<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Behind_the_scenes">Behind the scenes</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Neville_Longbottom?veaction=edit&amp;section=38" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Behind the scenes">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Neville_Longbottom?action=edit&amp;section=38" title="Edit section: Behind the scenes"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>

Vinyl">POP! Vinyl</a></p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<ul><li>Neville's initial lack of magical power could be deemed the result of his grandmother's overbearing presence as he acknowledges that she is constantly telling both him and others that he is not as talented as his parents and Dumbledore states that misery and lack of confidence can sap a wizard of his or her powers.</li>
<li>On <a href="/wiki/18_February" title="18 February">18 February</a>, Neville Longbottom's check-out of <i><a href="/wiki/Quidditch_Through_the_Ages" title="Quidditch Through the Ages">Quidditch Through the Ages</a></i> from the <a href="/wiki/Hogwarts_Library" title="Hogwarts Library">Hogwarts Library</a> ends.</li>
<li>Neville never took N.E.W.T. level <a href="/wiki/Transfiguration" title="Transfiguration">Transfiguration</a>, since he only earned an Acceptable. However, like Harry and Ron, he was still recruited by <a href="/wiki/Kingsley_Shacklebolt" title="Kingsley Shacklebolt">Kingsley Shacklebolt</a> into the <a href="/wiki/Auror" title="Auror">Auror</a> department after the battle to help track down any remaining <a href="/wiki/Death_Eaters" title="Death Eaters">Death Eaters</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-PotterCast_53-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-PotterCast-53">&#91;53&#93;</a></sup></li>
<li>It is possible <a href="/wiki/Severus_Snape" title="Severus Snape">Severus Snape</a>'s hatred for Neville was due to him being the second boy in the prophecy, which means if Voldemort had chosen to go after Neville rather than Harry, <a href="/wiki/Lily_J._Potter" title="Lily J. Potter">Lily</a> would still be alive.</li>
<li>There is a Feature named "Neville Longbottom, a true Gryffindor" on  <i><a href="/wiki/Pottermore" title="Pottermore">Pottermore</a></i>.</li>
<li>Rowling has revealed that the original last name for Neville's character was "Puff."<sup id="cite_ref-LEX_63-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-LEX-63">&#91;63&#93;</a></sup></li></ul>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 182px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/6/6a/NevilleLongbottomTCG.png/revision/latest?cb=20160120133540" title="Trevor">Trevor</a></p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<ul><li>In <a href="/wiki/J._K._Rowling" title="J. K. Rowling">J. K. Rowling</a>'s sketches of the five <a href="/wiki/Gryffindor" title="Gryffindor">Gryffindor</a> boys in <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter" title="Harry Potter">Harry Potter</a>'s year, Neville is shown as being the shortest,<sup id="cite_ref-LEX_63-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-LEX-63">&#91;63&#93;</a></sup> but in the films, Neville is the tallest, aside from <a href="/wiki/Dean_Thomas" title="Dean Thomas">Dean Thomas</a>. Rowling also described Neville as blond,<sup id="cite_ref-NPR_5-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-NPR-5">&#91;5&#93;</a></sup> but this was never printed in the novels, and in the films, he has brown hair.
<ul><li>Furthermore, it's unknown if his appearance changed as he matured over the years, but it should be noted that the film Neville grew from a short, chubby boy into a lean young man taller than even Harry.</li></ul></li>
<li>Neville is a playable character in <i><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Deathly_Hallows:_Part_2_(video_game)" title="Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows: Part 2 (video game)">Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows: Part 2 (video game)</a></i>.</li>
<li>In the <i><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Deathly_Hallows:_Part_2_(video_game)" title="Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows: Part 2 (video game)">Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows: Part 2 (video game)</a></i>, Neville deflects a curse sent from <a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle" title="Tom Riddle">Voldemort</a> using the <a href="/wiki/Sword_of_Gryffindor" title="Sword of Gryffindor">Sword of Gryffindor</a>, causing it to hit <a href="/wiki/Bellatrix_Lestrange" title="Bellatrix Lestrange">Bellatrix Lestrange</a> in the leg. This could have been to allow Neville payback towards Bellatrix for torturing his parents.</li></ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="In_films">In films</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Neville_Longbottom?veaction=edit&amp;section=39" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: In films">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Neville_Longbottom?action=edit&amp;section=39" title="Edit section: In films"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<ul><li>Neville is portrayed by <a href="/wiki/Great_Britain" title="Great Britain">British</a> actor <a href="/wiki/Matthew_Lewis" title="Matthew Lewis">Matthew Lewis</a> in the <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_(film_series)" title="Harry Potter (film series)"><i>film</i> adaptations</a>: <i><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Philosopher%27s_Stone_(film)" title="Harry Potter and the Philosopher&#39;s Stone (film)">Harry Potter and the Philosopher's Stone</a></i>, <i><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Chamber_of_Secrets_(film)" title="Harry Potter and the Chamber of Secrets (film)">Chamber of Secrets</a></i>, <i><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Prisoner_of_Azkaban_(film)" title="Harry Potter and the Prisoner of Azkaban (film)">Prisoner of Azkaban</a></i>, <i><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Goblet_of_Fire_(film)" title="Harry Potter and the Goblet of Fire (film)">Goblet of Fire</a></i>, <i><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Order_of_the_Phoenix_(film)" title="Harry Potter and the Order of the Phoenix (film)">Order of the Phoenix</a></i>, <i><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Half-Blood_Prince_(film)" title="Harry Potter and the Half-Blood Prince (film)">Half-Blood Prince</a></i> and <i><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Deathly_Hallows:_Part_1" title="Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows: Part 1">Deathly Hallows: Part 1</a></i> and <i><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Deathly_Hallows:_Part_2" title="Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows: Part 2">Part 2</a></i> and so is one of the 14 characters to appear in all 8 film adaptations.
<ul><li>Neville is portrayed to be left-handed. He is seen writing with this hand in a publicity photo for <i><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Order_of_the_Phoenix" title="Harry Potter and the Order of the Phoenix">Harry Potter and the Order of the Phoenix</a></i> and he also holds the <a href="/wiki/Sword_of_Gryffindor" title="Sword of Gryffindor">Sword of Gryffindor</a> in his left hand in publicity photos for <i><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Deathly_Hallows:_Part_2" title="Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows: Part 2">Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows: Part 2</a></i>. He is seen holding his <a href="/wiki/Neville_Longbottom%27s_wand" class="mw-redirect" title="Neville Longbottom&#39;s wand">wand</a> in his left hand several times in the movie series.</li>
<li>Since Matthew Lewis is from Leeds, West Yorkshire, he portrays Neville with a Yorkshire accent.</li>
<li>In a game of Mastermind, Matthew Lewis commented that he has been wearing a fat suit for most the films but in <i>Deathly Hallows</i>, he isn't going to be wearing it any longer (though the Neville character has been noticeably slimmer from the fourth film onward (except for <i>Order of the Phoenix</i>) which most likely is attributed to Neville's transition from shy and clumsy to a more hands-on supporting leader-like figure.)</li>
<li>Matthew Lewis' favourite line is "why is it always me?" from the <i>Chamber of Secrets</i>.</li>
<li>Matthew Lewis had to wear fake teeth for the fourth film.</li></ul></li>
<li>In the <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Goblet_of_Fire_(film)" title="Harry Potter and the Goblet of Fire (film)">film adaptation</a> of <i><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Goblet_of_Fire" title="Harry Potter and the Goblet of Fire">Harry Potter and the Goblet of Fire</a></i>, Neville is shown to be quite good at dancing, being one of the very last to leave the ball. However, in the novel, he is shown to be quite bad at dancing, stepping on Ginny's toes numerous times.</li>
<li>Also in the film adaptation of <i>Harry Potter and the Goblet of Fire</i>, it is Neville who gives Harry the Gillyweed before the Second Task, rather than <a href="/wiki/Dobby" title="Dobby">Dobby</a>, as he does in the book.</li>
<li>The short film <i><a href="/wiki/The_Queen%27s_Handbag" title="The Queen&#39;s Handbag">The Queen's Handbag</a></i> includes a reference to Neville's grandfather playing a trick on his grandmother in 1947. The canonicity of the mini-episode is uncertain.</li>
<li>In the <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Order_of_the_Phoenix_(film)" title="Harry Potter and the Order of the Phoenix (film)">film adaptation</a> of <i><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Order_of_the_Phoenix" title="Harry Potter and the Order of the Phoenix">Harry Potter and the Order of the Phoenix</a></i>, it is <a href="/wiki/Lucius_Malfoy" title="Lucius Malfoy">Lucius Malfoy</a> who breaks the prophecy, not Neville.</li>
<li>In <i><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Deathly_Hallows:_Part_2" title="Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows: Part 2">Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows: Part 2</a></i>:
<ul><li>There is a duel between Neville and <a href="/wiki/Scabior" title="Scabior">Scabior</a> during the <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_Hogwarts" title="Battle of Hogwarts">Battle of Hogwarts</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-64" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-64">&#91;64&#93;</a></sup></li>
<li>Neville confesses to Harry and Ginny during the battle that he is in love with <a href="/wiki/Luna_Lovegood" title="Luna Lovegood">Luna</a>. However, <a href="/wiki/Matthew_Lewis" title="Matthew Lewis">Matthew Lewis</a> has said that this is merely a "summer fling" before Neville marries <a href="/wiki/Hannah_Abbott" title="Hannah Abbott">Hannah Abbott</a> and Luna marries <a href="/wiki/Rolf_Scamander" title="Rolf Scamander">Rolf Scamander</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-65" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-65">&#91;65&#93;</a></sup></li>
<li>Neville is not burned by Voldemort, he instead makes a speech that despite Harry's 'death,' he still exists in their hearts, and that he didn't die for nothing. He even taunts Voldemort, saying that he will die in vain, (though Voldemort simply laughs at him), he pulls out the sword and Harry reveals himself to be alive. As the battle restarts, Voldemort, in his rage, actually <a href="/wiki/Stunning_Spell" title="Stunning Spell">stuns</a> Neville before he can give Harry the <a href="/wiki/Sword_of_Gryffindor" title="Sword of Gryffindor">Sword of Gryffindor</a> but he recovers and beheads <a href="/wiki/Nagini" title="Nagini">Nagini</a>.</li></ul></li></ul>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Notes_and_references">Notes and references</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Neville_Longbottom?veaction=edit&amp;section=42" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Notes and references">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Neville_Longbottom?action=edit&amp;section=42" title="Edit section: Notes and references
